Roosevelt's Mediation Succeeds, American Labor Strike Resolved 42

Labor-Management Agreement Established

Nation Overjoyed

(Washington) The White House has announced that the labor dispute in the automobile industry has been resolved after President Roosevelt convened leaders from both sides for consultation, and an agreement has been reached. The nation is overjoyed upon the release of this news. (Reuters, 25th)

(Washington) National Recovery Administration head Johnson made more optimistic remarks tonight, saying that although negotiations for the automobile industry dispute still face difficulties, they are largely ready, and he is confident that the labor strike can be quickly resolved. (Reuters, 25th)

(Washington) The resolution of the automobile industry dispute stipulates that workers have absolute freedom of collective bargaining, and they have the right to elect to be members of the company's union or a union affiliated with the American Federation of Labor. Federation of Labor President Green stated that workers have been guaranteed the right to organize themselves, engage in collective bargaining, and have the representatives they choose represent them. The President hopes that this agreement will lead to the creation of a factory administrative council, where workers can hold joint meetings with employers, creating a more equal relationship between labor and management. (Reuters, 25th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt issued a statement today, announcing the resolution of the automobile industry dispute, saying that "we have created a new path for the structure of American society." The key points of the new method are that a three-person administrative council will be established in Detroit within 24 hours, consisting of representatives from labor, management, and a neutral party, under the supervision of the National Recovery Administration. This council has the power to make final and binding judgments on issues such as dismissed workers and discrimination against workers, and can inspect various payrolls and lists of worker representatives. Union payrolls do not need to be submitted to the factory management, but failure to submit them will disqualify discrimination cases from being investigated. Currently, the labor side has appointed automobile industry employee Mr. Elder to participate as a representative of the council. (Reuters, 25th)

(Washington) The American automobile workers' strike, which has affected the entire country for the past three weeks, is now a thing of the past. At 7:45 p.m. this afternoon, the White House announced that the automobile industry labor strike has been resolved, which is generally considered satisfactory. Union leaders are not as optimistic about the terms of the agreement as the management side, as can be seen in their response to the President's initial declaration. According to the White House, this agreement is purely a compromise between labor and management. In this agreement, the President will appoint an arbitration committee composed of three members, with labor and management each having one member, and the other member being an outsider. The committee's task is to resolve various disputes that may arise in the future due to unfair treatment of worker representatives and the dismissal of workers. Union leaders had also requested to convene a workers' meeting and elect official representatives to negotiate with management, but this request has now been dashed. Reports from the Central and National Government Memorial Weeks 56

Shao Yuanchong: Three Recent Meetings

Dai Chuanxian: The Significance of Going to the Northwest

(Nanjing) The Central Committee held its 122nd Memorial Week at 9:00 am on the 26th. More than 400 people attended, including Ye Chucang, Shao Yuanchong, Wang Qi, Li Ciwen, Deng Jiayan, Li Zonghuang, Zheng Zhannan, and all staff members. Ye Chucang chaired the meeting. Shao Yuanchong reported that, in order to promote propaganda work, the Central Propaganda Committee recently convened three types of meetings in succession: literature and art, news, and film, in order to obtain a complete standard and policy for propaganda work. Regarding the literary and artistic meetings, because left-wing literature and art are currently popular in society, creating a decadent and romantic atmosphere, it is urgent to correct this. There are concrete discussions in this regard, and it is established that the Three Principles of the People will be the theoretical center of literary and artistic propaganda, nationalism will be the current policy of literary and artistic propaganda, and the content of literary and artistic propaganda works, etc. Regarding the news aspect, it stipulates the liaison of news, etc., and the communication policy, revises the Publishing Law, and decides on the method of severely cracking down on unscrupulous tabloids and newspapers that specialize in revealing social pathologies and corrupt events. Regarding the film aspect, the review authority of films has been unified and reorganized into the Film Inspection Committee. In the future, the copies will be reviewed before the companies make them, so as to avoid losses after the film is made, and to give the companies more convenience and reduce their difficulties and obstacles. Since convening three kinds of meetings, I feel that propaganda work is even more valuable, and it is especially necessary to concentrate our efforts. I hope that all comrades in the Central Committee and responsible comrades of party affairs in all parts of the country will contribute their time and ability to help, and the effectiveness of propaganda work can be seen immediately. Due to the drought years ago, the people of the province were displaced, and the tragic situation of death was too numerous to write down. The biggest cause of the drought is the failure to use water for irrigation. The amount of water in Shaanxi Province is not lacking. If water conservancy can be rectified, agricultural development will be very easy and drought can be avoided. Since the government has a plan to develop the Northwest, I plan to go to Shaanxi for inspection to prepare for the development. (Central News Agency, 26th)

Recently, the price difference between China and Germany was huge, so Huang was sent to the United States to ask experts for a public assessment, and it will be launched early next month. It is not going to the United States for inspection. 2. Yu went to Nanyang for inspection and is preparing his luggage. The travel date has not yet been decided. 3. The Central Machinery Factory was built with Geng money. The site in Caoxie Gorge is low-lying, and the cost of filling the base is about 190,000 yuan, which is not cost-effective. Now another site on the north bank of the Suzhou River in Shanghai has been designated as the construction site of the factory. 4. The Executive Yuan approved the allocation of 4.1 million yuan from this department to establish a newspaper factory. The plan has been sent to the Sino-British Geng Fund for review. A review meeting was held in Shanghai the day before yesterday, and it has been basically decided. It will be passed soon. (Special Dispatch, 26th)

It is negotiated to borrow money from the Central Geng Fund, and the association's review meeting yesterday can be decided next month. Decision on Connection Schedule Method

(Nanjing) The meeting on the joint transportation schedule of various routes across the country, 2

The meeting was held at the Ministry of Railways at 6 am. Chairman Yu discussed methods to facilitate passengers at the connection schedule of each route. The decision was: 1. All stations, large and small, on each route across the country will implement the sale of joint transportation tickets. 2. The end point of each route and the starting station of other routes are absolutely connected in time, so that passengers do not have to wait for a long time. 3. After getting off at the end point of Route A, the passengers' luggage will be specially delivered by special cars of each route to Route B connected to it. Each route has agreed to this principle and has studied the routes from Hangzhou to Beiping. Kailuan Coal Mine Strike Conditions Not Settled 70

Striking workers want rickshaw pullers to jointly strike

Public Security Bureau official beaten half to death while delivering orders

Workers underground nearly starve as mine entrances are surrounded

(Tianjin) Currently, only over three hundred coal miners at the Kailuan Tangshan mine are still insisting on not resuming work until the mine authorities fully accept their conditions. The striking workers convened a workers' congress on the 25th, but not many people attended, so a planned demonstration did not materialize. The striking workers issued slogans claiming that a stray bullet from police gunfire injured a rickshaw puller, hoping to get rickshaw pullers to jointly strike and expand the scale of the strike. On the evening of the 25th, an official from the Tangshan Public Security Bureau was ordered to deliver orders to the labor union and was dragged outside by the workers and beaten half to death. The detained secret service agent of the Public Security Bureau has not yet been released. Some in-shift workers who did not participate in the strike went underground to work. The striking workers, angry at their undermining of the strike group, surrounded the mine entrances, preventing anyone from sending food down the well. The underground workers, without food, stopped working and came out of the mine. Europe in the Midst of Tensions in International Relations (Paris Correspondence) 84

The Motives Behind the Italian-Austrian-Hungarian Economic Alliance

Many Thorns Still Lie Ahead for the Future of the Disarmament Issue

The uneasy atmosphere in Europe has made Europeans wary, fearing that a slight incident will trigger a disaster like that of 1914. Of course, we can still believe that although there are many current evils, a war will not break out immediately. There are many problems, and they are extremely serious. Taking France as an example, peaceful Paris has successively experienced riots that have only been seen since the Great Revolution. General social order is almost unsustainable. The cause originated from the market price issue in a small city in the southern region near Spain. As for involving the cabinet and many congressmen, although this is an ugly event that has been seen in French history, it is enough to prove the social unrest in Europe, especially the dark side of the relatively stable society of France, and the public's dissatisfaction with parliamentary politics.

During the same period that France was busy quelling internal disputes, the Austrian government and the Social Democratic Party also had very fierce street battles, with casualties exceeding one thousand. Moreover, the street battles in Vienna, this ancient city, are not like the protests of the citizens of Paris who are simply dissatisfied with internal affairs, merely exposing the ugliness of parliament. It is more than that. It contains very serious international problems, and of course also the contradictions of Austria itself. The international problem is the triangular opposition of Germany, France, and Italy. Germany wants to annex Austria, France is only consolidating its hegemony in Europe, and Italy has another idea, wanting to take advantage of the opposition between Germany and France to establish an economic alliance centered on Italy to confront Germany and France.

Of the 6.73 million people in Austria, 6.05 million are Austrian people of the German race. In Europe, in this fog garden where national consciousness is evident and national boundaries are strict, Austria has no economic outlet. France, insisting on the sanctity of treaties, is unwilling to provide Austria with economic assistance. In 1931, the German Foreign Minister Curtius and the Austrian Foreign Minister Schober signed the German-Austrian Customs Agreement. Although it was suppressed by the League of Nations, it was always the first smoke screen set for German-Austrian unification. On the one hand, France used the Treaty of Versailles and the Treaty of Saint-Germain as weapons to oppose this matter. On the other hand, the Czech Republic and Yugoslavia in particular fear that once Germany and Austria merge, the minority problem will inevitably become more fiercely contested. Even Italy fears that its 250,000 German-speaking people in South Tyrol will also be incited by the German National Socialist Party, causing serious disputes. Therefore, the Black Shirt Prime Minister sent his Deputy Foreign Minister Suvich to Budapest, the capital of Hungary, to visit Gömbös, and on February 24, he went from Budapest to Vienna to visit Prime Minister Dollfuss, who was clad in iron, to discuss the issue of how to form an economic alliance between Italy, Austria, and Hungary. It is said that in addition to striving to guarantee the independence of Austria and Hungary, Italy also suggested that Trieste and Fiume be used as maritime passages for Austria and Hungary, but on the condition that it opposes the National Socialist Party and maintains Austrian independence. Of course, maintaining Austrian independence has two meanings: one is not to merge with Germany, and the other is to stay away from France. This is naturally what Austria and Hungary are praying for. Originally, Austria was suffering from the competition of socialists, National Socialists, and fascists, to the point of not knowing what to do. France has to take into account the relationship of the Little Entente. In fact, the Little Entente countries now also have some discord with France, so Austria cannot seek help from France, nor can it accommodate Germany, so it has no choice but to listen to Italy's leadership.

However, after Austria and Hungary listen to Italy's orders, the political situation in Central Europe will become even more complicated. Germany, France, the Little Entente, Italy, Poland, and even the Soviet Union will be involved in certain places and at certain times. Of course, the United Kingdom cannot stand by either.

British Lord Privy Seal Eden visited France specifically after the formation of the Doumergue cabinet. The important issue to be discussed was to revive the disarmament conference, which had already become a zombie. In particular, he wanted to mediate the opposition between France and Germany. He successively exchanged opinions with Prime Minister Doumergue and other cabinet members, so that the friendly relations between Britain and France would continue for a long time. He visited German Chancellor Hitler on February 20 and President Hindenburg on the 22nd, also to discuss the disarmament issue. They only talked about how to be friendly and how to seek a consensus on disarmament opinions, but how to coordinate with France was not agreed upon. Eden went to Rome again on February 24 to visit Mussolini. Of course, there would be no huge differences between Britain and Italy, and there was more optimistic talk. Eden will leave Rome tomorrow to return to Paris to exchange views with the French authorities and then talk about how to resolve the disarmament issue.

However, another center of gravity has formed in Rome. If the economic alliance between Italy, Austria, and Hungary is really established, even if France can barely maintain its dominant diplomacy, it will be different from before. Austria and Hungary are united as a group, and the Little Entente countries will have to deal with it perfunctorily. As a result, France's opponents increase, diplomacy becomes more difficult, and the shock in Europe becomes even more severe. (February 26, 1934)

Song Ziwen Releases Details on the Cotton and Wheat Loan 85

丨Report to the Economic Conference丨

Song Ziwen, a standing committee member of the National Economic Council, recently released a report on the details of the US cotton and wheat loan and its implementation: "Last April, when Ziwen was ordered to attend the Washington Economic Discussion Conference, the Central Government, based on the Premier's industrial plan, instructed him to seize the opportunity to negotiate international investment. During the trip to the United States, he received a telegram instructing him on the principles and methods, and authorized him to handle the matter as the opportunity arose. Ziwen modestly acknowledged the instructions, and only hoped to exert his meager abilities to work diligently within the scope of not harming sovereignty, benefiting national finances, and being conducive to construction projects, so as not to fail in his mission.

After arriving in Washington, he proceeded to discuss with the US authorities based on this principle. However, the US government has no right to directly lend to the governments of other countries, and can only allow the US Reconstruction Finance Corporation to come forward to transfer the loan. According to the limitations of its organization, the company's loans to foreign countries are limited to agricultural products. The only agricultural products that are shipped to China in large quantities are cotton and wheat. According to China's customs reports, the number of US cotton and wheat imported over the years is very large.

During the negotiation period, he received a telegram from Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry stating that cotton prices in Shanghai were soaring, and raw materials were only borrowed for six weeks. Cotton mills were in a panic, so please discuss with the US to ship cotton to China as soon as possible. He also received a telegram from President Kong of the Central Bank stating that Rong Zongjing came to say that lending 600,000 bales of US cotton for resale to manufacturers to obtain funds to be used to help the rural areas and promote the cotton-growing areas will increase cotton production by 5 million dan per year, increasing farmers' income by 200 million yuan. The settlement price and interest will be handled in accordance with the wheat loan method, shipping 50,000 bales per month, completing the shipment in one year, including 420,000 bales of "7/8 inch," 120,000 bales of "15/16 inch," and 60,000 bales of "1 1/32 inch." If this can be done, it will be of great benefit to the finances. He hoped to proceed immediately. Subsequently, he received a telegram from Vice Minister Zou of the Ministry of Finance stating that President Wang wrote in a letter that the cotton textile mills in our country are becoming increasingly precarious. The biggest reason is that the domestic raw cotton is insufficient and its price is rising day by day, while the price of the produced products is falling due to the dumping of foreign goods. The way to save the situation is to ask the government to borrow money from the US government to purchase 600,000 bales of US cotton for resale to Chinese merchants' yarn mills, and use the money to help the rural areas, promote cotton-growing areas, and improve quality. After the matter was brought up for discussion in the Yuan, Chen Gongbo believed that it was beneficial and should be adopted, and was unanimously approved. Minister Song also had this idea, and instructed that the main points of the note and the opinion of the Yuan should be telegraphed to Junzuo immediately, requesting that negotiations be conducted with the US government to ensure success. The main points are: 1. The government should borrow 600,000 bales of US cotton from the US government. The settlement price and shipping method are the same as the US wheat loan. 2. 50,000 bales will be shipped from the US to China each month, and the shipment will be completed in twelve months. 3. This cotton includes 420,000 bales of 7/8-inch cotton, 120,000 bales of 15/16-inch cotton, and 60,000 bales of /38-inch cotton. 4. The interest is the same as US wheat. Subsequently, he received a telegram from Vice Minister Zou stating that the yarn mills only had enough cotton for one month, and requested that the foreign cotton tariff be waived for six months to purchase goods from the US and India; otherwise, they would stop work on July 1. Wu Tiecheng convened a meeting of the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and the banking community. The position of Minister Zou was that Rong Zongjing requested to borrow US cotton, and Junzuo was already proceeding with it, and it was possible to get relief; otherwise, we would discuss it later. Please telegraph the situation of the cotton shortage quickly. If it is difficult to achieve success temporarily, we will find other ways to provide relief, and so on. Ziwen repeatedly thought and considered that the existing industries in our country were already few and far between. Now the situation of the yarn mills is at a critical moment. At this time when the national situation is in danger, all industries are declining, the finances are exhausted, and the whole country is in panic, if even these yarn mills cannot be maintained, it will inevitably affect domestic finance. Then the so-called international economic cooperation and the hope of jointly developing China's industries are equal to nothing. Therefore, based on the instructions of the Central Government, the letters and telegrams of President Wang, Minister Chen, and President Kong, and the request of the factories, he made every effort to carry out the above-mentioned loan and promote its success. As for the quantity of cotton and wheat loans, it was based on the above-mentioned telegrams, with the national Chinese factories able to sell 600,000 bales per year as the standard. Therefore, the loan for the US cotton portion was 40 million US dollars (which can purchase more than 600,000 bales according to current market prices), while the US wheat and flour portion was only 10 million US dollars, which also far exceeded the above-mentioned borrowed amount according to the import statistics over the years.

As for the sales situation, according to the brief report of Xi Demao, manager of the US Loan Cotton and Wheat Affairs Office of the Central Bank: 1. The wheat loan of 6 million US dollars is about to be sold out, but the flour is still difficult due to market price relations. 2. Due to various reasons, only 10 million US dollars of cotton can be sold in this session. Therefore, the contract was revised with the United States as follows (the original contract has been published in various newspapers every year): (1) Under the item of the US wheat loan amount, 6 million US dollars, the term is extended from March 1 of this year to July 31 of the same year. (2) Under the item of the US flour loan amount, 4 million US dollars, the term is extended from March 1 of this year to December 31 of the same year. (3) Under the item of the US cotton loan amount, the amount is reduced from 40 million US dollars to 10 million US dollars. As for the US flour item, the Reconstruction Finance Corporation has the right to cancel it, but it must notify in advance. However, for the reduced portion of the US cotton loan amount, he worked hard to negotiate with the Reconstruction Finance Corporation to change it to purchase US wheat or other construction materials, but the company did not accept this proposal. Based on the above situation, the estimated revenue for this year is approximately 16 million yuan in national currency for the US wheat item, 5 million yuan for the US flour item, and 22.5 million yuan for the US cotton item, with a total net income of approximately 43.5 million yuan, which can be used for construction. This report is respectfully submitted for your consideration." Attached is the estimated revenue report from the manager of the US Loan Cotton and Wheat Affairs Office: "Respectfully submit the current revenue and expenditure status of the US loan cotton and wheat loan and the estimated total revenue in the future, divided into the following:

(1) After the loan contract is revised, the cotton and wheat loan amount should be changed as follows:

US Cotton US$10 million

US Wheat US$6 million

US Flour US$4 million

Total US$20 million

If the above loan amount can be used up completely, in addition to the principal amount for the first year, the total revenue will be approximately 48 million yuan in national currency.

(2) Current revenue and expenditure status: As of today, the price of all cotton and wheat that has been sold under the loan item and the accounts receivable for the sold cotton and wheat:

Revenue:

US Cotton 7.5 million yuan in national currency

US Wheat and Flour 19 million yuan in national currency

Expenditure:

Freight and handling fees, etc., approximately 3 million yuan in national currency

After offsetting revenue and expenditure, the remaining amount is 23.5 million yuan in national currency

(3) Estimated total revenue in the future: The sales of cotton and wheat are all handled according to market prices and have not suffered losses.

In addition to the above-mentioned total amount of 23.5 million yuan in national currency for the goods of the cotton and wheat that have already been sold, the revenue from the US cotton, US wheat, and US flour that have not been purchased and transported should be budgeted as follows:

1. US Cotton: As of today, a total of approximately 50,000 bales have been sold. If we consider the sales situation over the past six months, it will take approximately one year to complete the sales of the remaining US cotton. However, because the market inventory has not been abundant recently, there may be hope for a complete wholesale sale by the summer of this year.

Based on the estimated market price, the revenue from the sales of the remaining US cotton, in addition to the 7.5 million yuan in national currency that has already been received, is estimated to be approximately 15 million yuan in national currency based on the current exchange rate. 2. US Wheat: The total loan amount is 6 million US dollars, which can purchase approximately 320,000 short tons of US wheat. Assuming an average of 4 yuan per dan, and 60 yuan per ton, the revenue from 320,000 short tons of US wheat is approximately 19 million yuan. After deducting approximately 3 million yuan for freight, the net revenue from the sales of US wheat is approximately 16 million yuan in national currency.

3. US Flour: As of today, only 300 tons have been sold. The reason is that the office does not want to compete with domestic flour in the current domestic market with US flour, and the US authorities cannot agree with the world price. However, if the market needs it in the future and the price is suitable, we can purchase and sell it as much as possible. Then the estimated US flour item can have a surplus of 5 million to 10 million yuan in national currency. According to the above calculations, by the end of the year, it is estimated that there will be a net revenue of 22.5 million yuan in national currency from US cotton, 16 million yuan in national currency from US wheat, and 5 million to 10 million yuan in national currency from US flour, for a total of approximately 43.5 million to 48.5 million yuan in national currency. Xi Demao respectfully submits this report, March 24, 23rd year."

Second Installment of Victory Reports from the Sichuan Bandit Suppression Army 86

Liu Xiang Cables Chiang Kai-shek Reporting on Victorious Situation

Dispatching 50,000 Rounds of Bullets to Encourage Troops

Chengdu Dispatch: The Sichuan bandit suppression campaign has progressed rapidly since the second general offensive order was issued. One route, Deng's troops, captured the key towns of Wanghanba and Mumen. The second route, Tian's troops, captured the key towns of Duan'echang and Xinchang. The fourth route troops captured the key towns of Xiangtanzi. The fifth route army faced the main bandit force. On the left flank, Fan Shaozeng engaged in fierce battles with Xu bandits' troops around Shilong and Shie'e, killing over three thousand bandits. On the right flank, Yang Qiwen, Liao Zhen, Chen Houkun, and other units cleared the right bank of the Zhong River and are now joining forces with Tang Shizun and Xu Shaozong's divisions to encircle the pseudo-30th Army and pseudo-9th Army units at Luowenba. Yang Qin'an's independent regiment has already occupied the front of Jigongzui. The third route, Li's troops, have made even faster progress. After capturing Yanghe, the gateway to Bazhong, on the 14th, they advanced to the vicinity of Bazhong city. On the night of the 18th, they launched a surprise attack on Bazhong city. At that time, there were still over five thousand bandits in Bazhong. Li and Luo's troops encircled the city from the left and right. Three aircraft dispatched by the headquarters dropped bombs from the sky to assist in the battle, killing up to four thousand bandits. Few escaped. This occurred between the 18th and 19th. Liu Xiang, recognizing Luo's troops' efforts in suppressing bandits and their repeated meritorious deeds, not only issued a clear commendation order but also instructed the military department to allocate an additional 50,000 rounds of ammunition to encourage them. Yesterday, he telegraphed Nanchang to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, reporting on the gradual progress of each route of the bandit suppression army, the shrinking of the bandit areas, and the joint attack on Tongnan. The original telegram reads as follows: "Respectfully addressed to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of Nanchang: Since the issuance of the second phase of the Sichuan bandit suppression plan, various routes have engaged in numerous fierce battles and made steady progress. According to comprehensive intelligence from all sources, bandit leaders Xu Xiangqian, Chen Changhao, Zhang Guotao, and others have repeatedly held meetings, still intending to concentrate their main force to break through Xiadong, connect with He bandits, blockade the Yangtze River, and disturb Sichuan and Hubei. Evidenced by the rapid progress of the left flank and the fierce battles of the fifth route, their intentions and actions are clearly visible. Fortunately, the core troops of the bandits have already been dispersed among various units. The result of arbitrary slaughter has led to a loss of popular support. For a year, the manpower of Tongnanba has been exhausted. Therefore, incidents of responding to the government army and surrendering with weapons are heard daily. The people in the rear have saved on clothing and food to help, and the people close to the bandit areas have also transported supplies for us. Therefore, although after months of continuous fighting, morale remains as strong as ever. Recent offensives have been hampered by high mountains and dangerous roads, preventing significant progress. Our Deng's troops captured Puzi Ridge, Tian's troops captured Yinjiapu and Zhanggong Bridge, Luo's troops captured Enyang River on a cold day, and Qiao Wan recovered Bazhong. Li's troops captured Parrot Mountain, Yang's troops captured Lancao Ferry, Fan's troops captured Longfengchang, and Tang's troops captured Guandu Factory Stream. We are now ordering all units to continue the offensive along the entire line, setting a deadline to recover Tongjiang. Thanks to your virtue and the loyalty and bravery of the officers and soldiers, the bandit areas are gradually shrinking, and the time for encirclement and annihilation is not far off. Knowing of your concern, I hereby report. I humbly request that you issue instructions from time to time so that we may follow them. Respectfully, Liu Xiang, bowing and sealing." (National News Agency)

丨Special Commercial Intelligence Telegram from Reuters, March 26丨

Gold and Silver 88

London Gold Price: Today (26th), the London gold price is 136 shillings and 5 pence, up 2 pence from last Saturday.

London Silver Bars: Today (26th), the London silver price is 20 pence for spot and 20.0655 pence for forward, the same as last Saturday. The market is very quiet and unexciting.

New York Silver Bars: Today (26th), the New York silver market opened quietly but remained active with good sentiment because silver faction senators are about to add a new amendment proposed by Weller to the Dies proposal. Bulls expect agricultural and silver states to strongly support the new proposal to purchase an additional 750 million ounces of silver. Futures were unchanged or down two pounds, but the December contract rose 15 pounds from last Saturday's close.

Special Dispatch from London 89

Reuters, London, March 26: The British Financial News reports that the U.S. Treasury Department's refusal to allow domestic bankers to participate in French loans is of great importance, as it reveals the policy the U.S. authorities will adopt in the future. The war debt issue remains unresolved, preventing many borrowers from operating in the U.S. market. This situation is tantamount to the U.S. not being prepared to lend its export surplus to other countries, which will result in a continuous inflow of gold into the U.S., and European exchange rates will be under constant unfavorable pressure, which could endanger the stability of currencies at any time. Under these circumstances, attempting to stabilize the current inconvertible currencies would be a dangerous move.

Reuters, London, March 26: Professor Gregory, on behalf of the International Chamber of Commerce, stated in a memorandum that the decline in exchange rates is a tightening factor in world trade, rather than an inflationary factor as generally expected. There is no need to say that stabilizing currency prices will result in lower prices, nor is it necessary to say that the recovery of international lending depends on the stability of currencies. Experience shows that there must be some separation time between de facto stability and de jure stability. In his opinion, a conference should be convened to discuss this matter. The UK, Japan, the US, France, and Germany should join this conference. The purpose is to persuade President Roosevelt not to use his power to depress the price of the dollar, on the condition that the UK agrees to the existing US-UK exchange rate and the UK-Japan exchange rate.

The Tumultuous Politics of Japan (Tokyo Correspondence) 95

The Function of Parliamentary Politics is Completely Lost

Military Despotism Awaits the Future

Speculation on the Lifespan of the Saito Cabinet

Since Saito Makoto received the imperial order to form a cabinet, he has replaced five cabinet members in a row. The heads of the Navy, Army, Foreign Affairs, Commerce and Industry, and Education departments have all been replaced, with almost half of the cabinet members leaving office. According to common sense, the cabinet would have no reason not to collapse. Even if it is said to be a collaborative cabinet in times of emergency, there cannot be such a lack of linkage between cabinet members and between cabinet members and the entire cabinet body. Moreover, Japan still hangs the signboard of constitutional politics, and the parliament is still manipulated by the Zaibatsu behind the scenes. In other words, politics is still somewhat influenced by politics. Furthermore, the recent bribery scandal of Hatoyama Ichiro has superficially been glossed over. Hatoyama himself did not take bribes, but the ugliness of the political parties, whether it is the Seiyukai or the Minseito, is the same, exposed to the public. The credibility of parliamentary politics has been completely lost. At the same time, there have been twenty or thirty cases of schools in the education sector being prosecuted by the courts for bribery. Recently, the heads of the inspection and social education departments of the Tokyo Education Bureau were also prosecuted, and there is a tendency for this to expand in the future. This is not just a temporary stain on the Japanese government. From this prosecution, the ugly state of the Japanese education sector is exposed. It is said that to become an elementary school principal, if there is no financial power to mediate, then no matter how capable or hardworking you are, you will never have the hope of promotion. You can only be a teacher for the rest of your life and cannot develop your talents. Therefore, unfortunate incidents often occur in the Japanese education sector.

The problem of the decline of the rural economy also seems to have a subtle sign of improvement on the surface, but in reality, products are piled up like mountains. Not only is it not easy to reduce them at all, but there is also a tendency to increase them. For example, the price of rice, according to the calculation of the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, the production cost of each koku of rice is 23 yen and 34 sen, while the market price is only around 22 yen. After deducting transportation costs, it can be seen that it is difficult for rural life to have any hope of improvement in the short term. This is another reason for political instability and cabinet shake-ups in Japan.

Newspapers speculate that the Saito cabinet will collapse in the early summer of this year. The reason is that after the budget proposal is compiled, its mission is over. Furthermore, the general public dislikes it for being lifeless, and the military does not necessarily have to support it.

However, on the other hand, there is still the possibility of it continuing. First, in the Diet, the Minseito is at least a quasi-government party and expresses goodwill towards the current government. At the same time, it is wary of the arrogance of the military. It is feared that after Saito steps down, if either Konoe Fumimaro or Hiranuma Kiichirō comes to power, they will exhibit stronger military politics, and the political parties will inevitably suffer, and the Zaibatsu will inevitably be restricted. Second, although the relationship between the Seiyukai and Saito has gradually deteriorated, it is not yet so bad. Therefore, the Saito cabinet has a great possibility of prolonging its life. The third is a reason among insufficient reasons, that is, the problem of the successor after Saito steps down. It is quite difficult to find a suitable person at this time. Needless to say, a political party cabinet has no possibility of being realized. The person supported by the young officers is not liked by the Genrō (elder statesmen), and the Zaibatsu also opposes him. It is difficult to find a neutral, detached person who is stronger than Saito. Ugaki, Takahashi, and Kiyoura each have their weaknesses.

So, can Saito safely overcome the difficulties? This is another question. The reality is that Mr. Aomoto Shuzo, the former Vice-Minister of Railways and current member of the House of Peers, is pressing Mito Chuzo to establish a new railway. This can easily lead to the House of Peers impeaching political societies. Even if there is still a strong atmosphere in the House of Peers to let the Saito cabinet fulfill its responsibilities, once a branch issue occurs, and another cabinet member issue arises, the future is truly difficult to predict. Furthermore, the National League is indeed a minority party in the House of Representatives, and its power is also limited, but it has military connections behind it and has also developed relationships with right-wing groups. Therefore, its movement cannot be underestimated. It believes that two cabinet members of the same cabinet have simultaneously committed disciplinary violations, and this responsibility is not just for a certain cabinet member but for the entire cabinet. Therefore, it wants to propose a vote of no confidence, at least to expose the stains of the current cabinet as much as possible, thereby creating a bad atmosphere in the House of Peers and triggering public antipathy. If the Saito cabinet cannot satisfactorily resolve the work of supplementing the positions of education chiefs after the Diet session ends, then the lifespan of the current cabinet will truly be difficult to prolong (March 9).

Qingdao Municipal Government Reliefs Native Produce Exports 96

Strictly Prohibiting Speculation, Hoarding, and Profiteering

Qingdao Dispatch: Mayor of Qingdao Shen Honglie, due to the sluggish sales of Shandong native products and the plight of merchants, in order to provide relief, had previously requested the central government via Governor Han Fuqu of the Shandong Provincial Government to reduce export tax rates to assist the export of native products, and also advised Qingdao capitalists to raise funds to organize a Puli company to specialize in purchasing raw rice and exporting it overseas. Also, fearing that unscrupulous merchants would take the opportunity to hoard and manipulate prices, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau was ordered to investigate and register the quantity of native products currently in the city. Imported goods must also be registered with the Social Affairs Bureau, prepared for export overseas, and not allowed to be sold locally. After this adjustment, the market greatly enlivened. The quantity of raw rice exported from March 2 to March 21 has reached more than 11,400 tons (approximately 862,000 yuan). The Puli company has purchased more than 40,000 bags, approximately 3,600 tons, which can be shipped out in early April. Other businesses engaged in overseas exports are buying raw rice on a large scale, preparing to export it overseas during the tax reduction period. According to the Social Affairs Bureau's investigation, the quantity of native products currently stored in the city includes more than 449,000 bags of raw rice, more than 37,000 bags of peanuts, and more than 18,600 baskets of raw oil. Just taking raw rice as an example, approximately 100,000 bags have been exported, and the 300,000 bags still stored in the city can also be shipped out in the shortest possible time. However, during this period, it is difficult to guarantee that there will be no speculative unscrupulous merchants hoarding and profiteering or arbitrarily manipulating the situation. It is imperative to take precautions and strictly prohibit them. The Ministry of Finance has also received reports that there are many such speculators in Qingdao, asking the municipal government to pay attention. The municipal government has issued a notice to the municipal chamber of commerce to instruct the exchange and various native product merchants to comply. The text of the municipal government's order to the municipal chamber of commerce is recorded as follows: "Approved Ministry of Finance consultation opened, regarding Qingdao, Jinan, Weihaiwei, Yantai and other places, within a fixed period of three months, to export peanuts, raw peanut kernels, peanut oil reported overseas, should be given a 61% reduction in export tax according to the original export tax rate. The Ministry had previously ordered the customs to comply and consulted your municipal government for reference, originally because peanut kernels are a major export of our country and also the main agricultural product of Shandong Province, which has a significant impact on the livelihood of farmers and local finance. Your municipal government has also repeatedly requested relief in response to the current plight of farmers and businesses, and the Ministry is willing to sacrifice tax revenue to implement the above-mentioned tax reduction measures to show its joint support for the export of native products. However, according to investigation reports, speculators in Qingdao are using the miscellaneous grain exchange as a place to profit, hoping that the market price of overseas peanuts will rise, so that the peanuts they purchased can have surplus profits to fulfill their desires for speculation and profiteering. Even bankers and people who have nothing to do with the production and sale of peanut kernels have joined this gambling transaction in order to try their luck. Bank loans are not guaranteed by reliable export contracts, but must have actual goods as collateral. As a result, local market prices are so high that they exceed the prices of Indian and Dalian products opened overseas. The inability of Shandong peanut kernels to be exported is greatly related to this unnatural environment. The Ministry believes that reducing tax donations to reduce the cost of peanut kernels is originally intended to adapt to foreign market prices, so as to maintain the status of foreign trade and relieve the livelihood of farmers. Those who have nothing to do with the production and sale of peanut kernels are manipulating the market by means of speculation and profiteering, causing the local price of peanut kernels to rise. Farmers have not enjoyed the benefits of this price increase, and the export of peanut kernels is adversely affected as a result, which is obviously contrary to the government's original intention of relief. How to restrict speculators based on the production situation of peanut kernels and the original price of production areas is a matter of farmers' interests and foreign trade. In addition to consulting separately, it is appropriate to consult your municipal government to consider and handle it and reply to He et al. Approved here, check this matter has been convened each merchant to explain earnestly, and has ordered the Social Affairs Bureau strictly prohibit the record, since the former by, Yingdang followed suit, if each native produce merchants still have intentional speculation hoarding profiteering circumstances, the government will strictly investigate and prohibit, never connivance, in addition to consulting the reply, should go to make the Association transferred to the exchange and various native produce merchants comply, this order. " (March 24)

Chaoshan Relief Financial Measures 97

Commercial Banknote Total Amount Increased to Ten Million

City Chamber of Commerce Decides on Issuance Measures

Shantou Dispatch: Chaoshan financial exhaustion. The provincial government previously decided to approve the issuance of 4 million yuan of commercial banknotes to provide relief. However, there were internal differences of opinion within the chamber of commerce. Due to the uneven distribution of Chaoyang Chenghai gangs, the issuance of commercial banknotes caused great obstacles. Matters such as the resignation of Chen Shaowen and the fraudulent election of members have been discovered repeatedly. Financial relief is increasingly impossible, industry and commerce are in distress, and all industries are in depression. East District member Li Yangjing once expressed the need to persuade business leaders to sacrifice their prejudices and work together to overcome the difficulties. On the 14th, the City Chamber of Commerce welcomed Li Yangjing to the meeting for guidance. When Li arrived at the Chamber of Commerce, he persuaded the representatives, saying that the commercial banknotes had been approved by the provincial government and should be implemented as soon as possible to provide relief. As a result, business leaders were very willing to unite and cooperate so that the commercial banknotes could be issued as soon as possible to provide relief. Eight items were immediately decided: (1) Ask the provincial government to exempt the deposit of 20% of central banknotes when issuing banknotes. (2) Increase the total amount of commercial banknotes to 10 million yuan. (3) Change the face value of commercial banknotes to 100 yuan and 200 yuan, two types. (4) The 1.9 million yuan of guaranteed white notes, auxiliary banknotes, and guarantee slips issued by various silver shops must be fully recovered within one month after the issuance of commercial banknotes. As for the 3 million yuan of guaranteed banknotes, they must also be fully recovered within six months after the issuance of commercial banknotes. (5) The price of industrial property to guarantee the issuance of commercial banknotes, the original regulations stipulated that the house will be calculated at 70%, but in order to avoid the deposit of 20% of the Chinese currency, the foundation of the banknote should be stable so as not to cause danger, so the industrial property of houses guaranteed to issue commercial banknotes will be calculated at 50%, and the land will be calculated at 40%. As the price of Haitan land is lower, for fear of fraud, it should not be guaranteed. (6) The price of the exchanged guaranteed industrial property should be re-evaluated, because the price of industrial property depends on the rise and fall of the market price. (7) The exchange of industrial property should be approved by the full committee. (8) The articles of association for the issuance of commercial banknotes originally stipulated a weekly interest rate of 2%, which will be used as funds. However, the funds should be frugal, and the weekly interest rate should be changed to 4%, which should be paid in two periods per year. Each period should be divided into six months, with 5% of the funds being used for the association's expenses and 95% being saved for the business bank that issues the commercial banknotes to deduct it when it is recovered in the future. That is, if a business bank issues 10,000 yuan of commercial banknotes, the weekly interest rate is 4%, and the annual interest payable is 400 yuan. Of these 400 yuan, 5% will be used for expenses (i.e., 20 yuan), and the remaining 3.8 million will be saved by the association. If the interest paid is in commercial banknotes, 5% will be withdrawn, and the remaining 95% will be destroyed. If cash is paid, it will be used as the bottom when it is recovered in the future (i.e., 100 yuan of commercial banknotes issued should pay 400 yuan of current ocean interest. In addition to 20 yuan for expenses, only 9,620 yuan will be recovered in the future, because the owed 380 yuan has been offset by the interest paid). Regarding the above eight items, Li Yangjing has requested the provincial government to adopt them as appropriate. If the amount of 10 million yuan can be issued, the Chaoshan financial situation can be expected to find a solution. (18th)

Liu Gui Tang's Remnants Fled Back to Bao Du Mountain 98

Lu Army's Encirclement and Suppression Suffered Heavy Casualties

Han Fu Ju Returned to Ji'nan from Jieshou

Ji'nan Correspondence: Liu Gui Tang's remnant bandits in the Wen Shang area, after being fiercely attacked by government troops and suffering heavy losses, deeply realized that the provincial army's defenses were tight along the Jinpu Railway south of Tai'an. They changed their strategy and split into two groups, fleeing north, one entering Pingyin and the other running to Feicheng. By the evening of the 23rd, they fled east again, approaching the Jinpu Railway line, hoping to cut off the railway east from the area north of Tai'an, from Shou Wande to Zhangxia. Han Fu Ju immediately dispatched troops to intercept them, ordering Sun Tongxuan to station troops in Wande, leading the pistol battalion, engineering battalion, and Zhang Deyin's regiment of the 81st Division's Zhan Shutang, to block and attack along the road. Han also personally went to Jieshou to command, and fierce battles broke out overnight near Wande. Liu's bandits, by this time, felt that they were at the end of their rope, so they decided to make a final struggle, dividing into several small groups of thirty or fifty to sixty people each. Starting at three o'clock this morning (the 24th), they began to flee across the Jinpu Railway from Jieshou Wande, north of Tai'an, in separate groups. Government troops resolutely counterattacked, and Dai Hongbin also commanded armored vehicle teams to patrol and encircle, killing many bandits and capturing countless camels. However, because most of Liu's bandits were cavalry, they desperately fled. As a result, all the remaining bandits fled east across the railway. By dawn this morning, there was no trace of the bandits. The bandit force, estimated to be still over a thousand people, all fled towards the Meng Mountain area. Han Fu Ju, believing that since Liu's bandits had crossed the railway, they would certainly flee back to their old nest in the Meng Mountain and Bao Du Mountain area of southern Shandong, immediately ordered the 81st Division's Yun Qichang brigade and the 74th Division's Ma Guanyi brigade to be responsible for pursuing Liu's remaining bandits, ordering them to completely eliminate the bandits within a month. The headquarters also issued a wireless radio to each brigade to facilitate communication. The Yun Qichang brigade arrived at Jieshou and disembarked, and the Ma Guanyi brigade also took three trains from Da Wenkou and disembarked at Tai'an to join the Yun brigade and advance east to pursue and suppress Liu's bandits.

Han Fu Ju, believing that Liu's bandits had fled east, returned to Ji'nan by train from Jieshou at eleven o'clock this morning. According to Han, after being encircled and suppressed by the provincial army, Liu Gui Tang's bandit force had fled in disarray. The remaining bandits, estimated to be over a thousand people, had crossed the railway eastward at three o'clock this morning, and it was predicted that they would flee back to their old nest in Bao Du Mountain in southern Shandong. The Yun Qichang brigade and the Ma Guanyi brigade had been dispatched to pursue them, hoping to annihilate them in the shortest possible time.

Last night (the 23rd), due to the congestion of military trains in the area north of An, the 301st through train from Peiping to Shanghai and the 3rd train from Jinpu to Pukou were both blocked in Ji'nan. This morning, the 302nd through train from Peiping to Shanghai from the south was also stopped in Xuzhou and dared not head north. Also, the 1st train from Peiping to Pukou from the north was blocked after arriving in Ji'nan at 9:20 and could not head south. A total of three trains were stopped at the Ji station, and north-south traffic was cut off. It was not until 10:00 this morning that the military trains in the Jieshou area cleared the way, and the trains blocked in Ji'nan gradually headed south (24th).

Songjiang: The Weng Surname Robbery Case Cracked, Culprit Apprehended 99

Weng Weiqing's family, a resident of the Xuantan Temple Township in Pudong, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits on the night of March 7th this year. Each bandit was armed with a deadly weapon and broke into the house, tying up the victim, Weng Weiqing, and his son, Weng Xiding. The bandits burned off the victim's beard and beat him, causing him to fall to the ground groaning in pain. The bandits then swarmed into the house one after another, arbitrarily looting before leaving. Afterward, the water and land police teams rigorously investigated and arrested Chen Caisheng, a suspect in the case, near Shengzi Temple. He confessed to the robbery at the scene and also implicated several accomplices. After verifying his confession, the team detained the suspect for further questioning. Yesterday, another team was dispatched to the countryside to arrest the remaining suspects.

Suzhou: Lu Fusheng is a Prime Suspect in the Assassination Case in Jiaozhi West Market 100

Ma Fushou, a resident of No. 73 Shangtang, West Market, Jiaozhi, was a man of modest means. He had a younger sister who married Lu Fusheng (also known as Ma Fusheng) from the same town. On the night of November 23rd of the previous year, Fushou, his mother Zhou, his wife Wang, and his eleven-year-old son, A Jin, went to a wedding banquet at the Zhang family, relatives less than half a li away, at the Huitan Temple. After the banquet ended at seven o'clock, Fushou and his wife took their son home first. At two o'clock in the morning, their hired worker, Chen Hongsheng (who was helping at the Zhang family), returned home with Ma's son-in-law, Fusheng. They parted ways midway. When Chen arrived at the Ma house, he found the row gate unlocked. Upon entering, he discovered that Fushou, his wife, and his son, A Jin, had all been murdered in their beds. The case has remained unsolved for a long time. Xie Guoan, the chief of the responsible Public Security 7th Branch, recently learned that when Ma's son-in-law, Lu Fusheng, was interrogated by local authorities after the incident, he had handed a package wrapped in newspaper to villagers Yang Azhao, A Jinshou, and A Yinsheng, asking them to discard it in the river. Yang opened the package and found two sharp knives inside with yellow bloodstains. On New Year's Eve of the previous year, he borrowed money from Fusheng, who gave him a rice husking bed worth six silver dollars. It was also learned that Ma Fushou's mother, Zhou, had given part of her farmland to her son-in-law, Fusheng, so she often stayed at her son-in-law's house. Zhou had a hidden cache of four thousand yuan, and it was rumored that Fusheng had dug it up after the incident. On the 25th, Yang Azhao, A Jinshou, A Yinsheng, and Lu Fusheng were taken into custody. The district head, town head, and local bailiffs were summoned to investigate the cache at the Ma house. As a result, three large earthenware jars were unearthed. One was empty and discarded on the ground, while the other two were buried deep in the soil. One contained soil and 104 silver dollars, and the other contained 1,128 silver dollars. In addition, Zhou had recently sold forty mu of land for 2,196 silver dollars, but the money could not be found. Lu Fusheng, the prime suspect, was handed over to the Public Security Bureau yesterday (the 26th). After questioning the witnesses, Yang Azhao and others, who confessed to the above, Lu Fusheng admitted that the two knives were indeed his, but he asked Lu and others to dispose of them out of fear of suspicion. He has not confessed to the murders.

Construction of the Suzhou-Changzhou Highway Begins 101

The Suzhou-Changzhou Highway is now scheduled to begin construction next month. Yesterday (the 26th), Yu Liqi, the director of the Engineering Office, came to Suzhou from Zhenjiang and went to Lumu for inspection. The office decided to set up an office in Changshu, with Pan Siqian in charge, and a branch office in Likou Jiejing. The road will have a total of 24 bridges, 13 culverts, and 60 ditches. It was originally planned to be built through conscripted labor, but due to the busy farming season, it was feared that there would be no good results, so it was changed to a contract system. Bids are scheduled to be opened on April 2nd, construction will begin on the 10th, and it is scheduled to be completed by mid-June for long-distance traffic.

Wuxi: The Pingmin Xi Yi Institute Incident Resolved 102

At the Pingmin Xi Yi Institute in our city, in the late night of the 23rd of this month, an apprentice, Xia Shengbao, suddenly committed suicide due to severe stress. The remaining apprentices were all indignant and rioted, destroying the sanitation room and beating Director Wu and others, as reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that since the institute was established in 1929, it has been poorly managed and riddled with corruption. The apprentices were treated very harshly, even to the point of being unable to eat their fill, worse than prison inmates. When working in the workshop, they were whipped for the slightest mistake. As for wages, they received only a few cents per month, and even that was not always paid. Recently, apprentice Xia Shengbao contracted typhoid fever and was very ill. He requested medical treatment from the personnel department, but the personnel department said harshly, "Why ask for a doctor? No one has died in this institute for a long time, and there are several coffins piled up." Xia Shengbao, severely affected by this, committed suicide. When the apprentices heard this news, they rioted. At nine o'clock yesterday morning, County Magistrate Yan personally went to the institute to investigate and summoned all the apprentices for a lecture, warning them not to cause any more trouble. At that time, the apprentices also explained their suffering to County Magistrate Yan, requesting three improvements to the institute: 1. The apprenticeship period for general apprentices should be shortened to one year, and the apprenticeship period for special apprentices should be shortened to four months. 2. The apprentices' meals should be improved to meet sanitary standards. 3. Qian Laosi, who was beaten by the director during the disturbance, should be sent out for medical treatment. County Magistrate Yan agreed to find ways to improve these things. The apprentices were satisfied and returned to the workshop to work as usual. Xie Wenhua, Yang Ahong, Wang Ruming, and the other three apprentices who caused the trouble were sent to the county government for questioning. The order in the institute is now maintained by more than eighty police officers and more than ten police officers from the Third Branch, who are armed day and night to maintain order. At the same time, Pingmin Institute Chairman Qian Qing and Wu Bangzhou discussed the aftermath with County Magistrate Yan. It was decided that those who have learned enough to support themselves will be released as appropriate. Those who are from local families and are being taken care of should notify their parents to come to the institute to take them back within three days to avoid further trouble. The special department will be disbanded immediately. It is rumored that Zou Tongyi will be hired as the director.

Court Orders Gu Renfa to Appear for Questioning 103

Liu Zhuo, the former chief of the Second Public Security Bureau, and his wife, Wen Rongzhen, were arrested and imprisoned for resisting transfer and obstructing official duties. The case also involved Su Province Civil Affairs Director Gu Renfa's wife, Li Shuyun, and her daughter, who were also arrested in Shanghai and sent to Wuxi for interrogation. It is now learned that after the County Court Prosecutor's Office investigated the case according to law, it determined that there was no evidence of Li Shuyun selling official positions and collecting money, so it did not need to investigate. It only focused on the part of obstructing official duties. The court sent a letter to the County Public Security Bureau a few days ago, requesting that the seized evidence be sent to the court for verification. Chief Li approved the letter and sent the eight pieces of evidence related to Li Shuyun found in Liu Zhuomin and his wife's luggage to the court. However, Li Shuyun denied sending a letter to Liu's wife and requested to compare handwriting. Yesterday, the court received two more pieces of evidence from the Civil Affairs Department, claiming that Li Shuyun was engaging in fraud. After Qian, the chief judge, reviewed them, he determined that the evidence was insufficient to prove that Li Shuyun had committed fraud and collecting money. Moreover, Li Shuyun is Director Gu's wife, and Director Gu is the informant in this case. According to criminal procedure, it is necessary to order Gu Renfa to appear in court for questioning. Chief Judge Qian and President Xu discussed it and decided to send a telegram to Chen Guofu, the chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, to forward it to Gu, as Gu is now in Jiangxi and it is difficult to send a summons. The telegram was sent that evening, and the original text read, "Please order Gu Renfa to bring evidence and come to court for questioning in person," etc. It is not known whether Gu Renfa will respect the national judiciary and come to Wuxi to surrender for questioning. As for Li Shuyun, since being detained in the detention center, she has suffered excessive stress and developed a severe stomach ailment, with alternating chills and fever, moaning in prison, and the situation is very tragic. Li Wenhui, Li Shuyun's uncle, visited her a few nights ago, and Shuyun complained a lot and couldn't help but sigh. Liu Zhuomin's second son, Zhuxin (10 years old), who has fallen into a foreign land, also fell ill in the hostel yesterday. Also, after Yan Shenyu, the magistrate of this county, angrily resigned from his position due to this case, telegrams from all walks of life were sent to the province requesting his retention, flying like snowflakes. Yesterday, the County Party Department, the County Property Office, the Municipal Management Committee, the County Chamber of Commerce, and the County Farmers' Association organized the Agricultural Workers' Union and the Silk Factory Industrial Workers' Union, all sending telegrams to retain him. However, Magistrate Yan's resignation is firm. Although the provincial government issued an order of consolation and retention, his attitude is negative. Yesterday (the 26th), he continued to submit a second letter of resignation to the provincial government. The original telegram read, "Chairman Chen and Director Gu of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the previous telegram of resignation has been received. Shenyu has stated the circumstances sincerely. Recently, I have been overworked and feel increasingly physically exhausted. Wuxi is located in an important area, and it is also at a time of reorganization of the police force and re-division of districts. The political affairs are complicated and I am afraid of causing delays. I beg you to approve my request as soon as possible and select someone to take over. I am extremely apprehensive and await orders." Yan Shenyu, Magistrate of Wuxi County, respectfully begs for forgiveness.

Changzhou: The Fifteenth District Repeatedly Apprehends Bandits 104

The Fifteenth District Office and the Second Public Security Bureau of Wuyi County, believing that the Han Zong Nunnery in the Bajiao Township of their jurisdiction had previously been the scene of a robbery, conducted separate investigations and apprehended Wu Jinyuan, one of the bandits involved in the case. He was brought before the county government for questioning, and he confessed to the robbery and said that there were still accomplices at large. The Fifteenth District Office and the Second Public Security Bureau then conducted further investigations. Recently, He Wenquan, the leader of the Seventh Jia of the Bao Wei, learned that He Tingwei, a wanted suspect in the case, had been hiding outside and had now returned. He sent militiamen to arrest him and brought him to the district for preliminary interrogation. The suspect confessed to robbing Han Zong and admitted to spending the stolen goods. He was recorded his confession, and the suspect was sent to the county for questioning yesterday (the 25th).

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes a Large Quantity of Anti-Japanese Goods 105

Jin Jiwen, the inspection director of the Wuyi Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, led inspectors and passed by Baijia Bridge outside the East Gate on the 25th. Seeing a cargo ship, they boarded it for inspection. After a detailed examination, they found a box of anti-Japanese shuttles, totaling 200, transported by the Shanghai Jinchang Iron Factory to the Changzhou Lida Cloth Factory, and a piece of anti-Japanese shuttles, totaling 100, transported by the Shanghai Xiangchang Organization Hardware Store to the Changzhou Lida Cloth Factory. There were also five bundles of suspected anti-Japanese yarn spools of various sizes. All the goods were brought to the association. It is heard that the shuttle part is definitely anti-Japanese goods. The yarn spools will be handled after identification.

Zhenjiang: Yida & Co. Careless 106

Yida ginseng shop on Tianzhutang Street in this port has been open for more than ten years. At about 5:00 p.m. on the 25th, the electric wire caught fire, and the fire spread to the house. Fortunately, the fire brigade arrived in time to put out the fire, and only one row of cargo rooms was burned down. The shop has tens of thousands of yuan in fire insurance, so the loss is small.

Yangzhou: Jiangdu will Establish a Local Court 107

The people of Jiangbei believe that Jiangbei is vast and transportation is obstructed, and there is a real need to establish a local court to facilitate litigation. Therefore, when Justice Minister Luo inspected Yangzhou two months ago, representatives from all walks of life repeatedly petitioned Luo. It is heard that a local court will soon be established in Yangzhou. However, according to detailed investigations, it is completely different from the nature of the above-mentioned additional local court. Because the central government plans to adopt a three-level, three-trial system, all county courts in the country will be abolished uniformly. In the future, the first trial will be held in the local court, and its jurisdiction will be based on the county as a unit. Therefore, although the name of the Jiangdu Branch is elevated, the actual judicial power is reduced. The hope of the people here to add a local court above the county court is probably hopeless. However, it is hoped that the judicial authorities will set up a higher branch court within the territory of Yangzhou to avoid the hardships of litigants traveling.

Nantong: Strictly Prohibit Police Officers from Protecting Opium and Narcotics 108

Tongyi has strictly banned opium and narcotics. A large number of drugs are still imported from time to time. The opium dens in the city and countryside are still operating. County Magistrate Cheng ordered Fu Qianzhi, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, to investigate and ban them effectively, and strictly ordered the police officers of each district not to receive bribes and protect them.

Tongtai Haiqi Special Police Commander 109

In order to protect themselves from bandits, the industrial and reclamation companies in Jiangbei have submitted a request to the Civil Affairs Department to organize three special industrial police teams to be stationed in nine counties, including Tongtai Haiqi. They are now planning to facilitate their command. A special police headquarters for Tongtai Haiqi has been established in Nantong, with Hong Junqing as the commander.

Jiashan: Farmers' Riot Caused by Conscription of Strong Men 110

Since receiving the order from the Provincial Security Department of our county to compile the first phase of the reserve team, the district offices of our county have sent personnel to the towns and villages under their jurisdiction to start the compilation, so that they can be sent to the county for training as soon as possible. Unexpectedly, the ignorant farmers all held a timid concept. The strong men who were drafted cried and begged to be exempted, while the brave ones stubbornly resisted. Yesterday, the farmers in the countryside near the Da Ningzhuang Town in the county planned to draft strong men for future combat use. As a result, five or six hundred people gathered and swarmed to the district office, destroying all the tables, chairs, and utensils, and burning all the documents and books. The district head, Lu Baozhi, and the staff of the office all fled to escape and were able to escape safely. Later, Ji Dasheng, the head of the village, knelt down and kowtowed countless times to the farmers before they all retreated. The Public Security Bureau initially sent police to suppress the riot, but seeing five or six hundred farmers, drunk and crazy, and difficult to suppress, they retreated. For a time, the city was alarmed and the order was in chaos.

Water Police Assaults and Injures Boat Owner 111

The Qingtai steamship of Wang Qingji Steamship Bureau in Xiadianmiao Town of our county travels to Zhouzhuang and Liji. The other day, the steamship returned to port from Suzhou. The patrol boat of the Fifth Water Police Team was at the port, and the stern of the steamship collided with the patrol boat, knocking over the patrol boat's stove and sundries. All the patrolmen on the ship rushed to the steamship, dragged the steamship owner ashore, and beat him severely. As a result, the sailors on the steamship also resisted the patrolmen. Although the patrol captain and local merchants tried to persuade them, it was ineffective. Fortunately, the leader of the security backbone team sent team members to report to Captain Wang of the Water Police, and the two sides worked together to suppress the situation before it subsided.

Hangzhou: Old Public Debt Redemption Lottery 112

The sixth redemption lottery for the old public debt of Zhejiang Province was held at the City Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 p.m. today (26th). Tang Shijian, a section chief of the Department of Finance, was sent to preside over the lottery. The winning numbers for the first group were "10", for the second group "25", for the third group "59", for the fourth group "77", and for the fifth group "96". The winning tickets will be redeemed and the second interest will be paid from April 1st of this year. The Hangzhou China Bank, Zhejiang Local Bank, and the county treasury are designated as the redemption information agencies. This is hereby announced.

Lu Diping's Old Illness Relapses 113

Lu Diping, the chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, has been overworked in presiding over the provincial government. His health has not fully recovered since his illness last year. At 8:00 p.m. on March 22nd, Lu took a car to the private residence of Yang Mianzhong, a member of the Provincial Government Committee, on Changsheng Road to discuss political affairs. At about 9:00, he suddenly felt dizzy and was immediately treated by Chinese and Western doctors. The next day, he telegraphed to Shanghai to invite Dr. Le Wenzhao to Hangzhou for diagnosis and treatment. According to the doctor, it was a recurrence of his old illness due to overwork, and he has made great progress in recent days, eating milk and bread every day. When Lu fell ill, Yang Mianzhong telegraphed Nanchang to report his condition to Chairman Chiang. Today, Chiang replied by telegram, instructing Lu to rest and recuperate. Lu has telegraphed to the Central Executive Yuan to request a one-month leave for recuperation. His duties will be taken over by Lu Bichou, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs. Lu is currently being treated in Yang's residence.

Local News

Tang Youren Discusses Diplomatic Events 114

The North China Relationship is a Problem for the Entire China

The Entire Country Should Pay Attention

Central News Agency: Tang Youren, the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, went to Peiping to inspect the situation in North China. He has now returned to Nanjing after completing his official duties. He arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing the morning before yesterday and is scheduled to return to Nanjing on Wednesday. After visiting President Wang, he will go to Wuhan to inspect and represent President Wang to comfort Shi Ying, the mayor of Beijing, who is staying in Wuhan. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Tang at his residence yesterday morning to inquire about diplomatic issues. According to his talk, it is as follows.

North China Disaster Victims Awaiting Relief 115

According to Tang, his trip to Peiping and Tianjin was purely to inspect the real situation in North China, and there were no important tasks. The rumors circulating have already been denied, and such rumors are not worth the attention of knowledgeable people. The situation in North China is extremely complex, not a local problem for North China, but a problem for the entire country. The entire country should pay attention to it. Tang also said that when he passed through Tianjin, he saw a large number of refugees coming and going on the streets, and the situation was extremely painful. It is necessary to find ways to provide relief immediately, as this is related to the problem of public security in North China.

Huang Fu is About to Go South 116

Tang continued, Huang Yingbai, the chairman of the North China Political Affairs Reorganization Committee, will soon go south from Peiping to return to his hometown of Songjiang to sweep the tombs of his ancestors. He will stay in Nanjing for a short time. Tang said that he had not heard of the Japanese news reports that the Japanese envoy, Arima Akira, would meet with Huang in Nanjing. It may be a speculation, or it may not be known.

British Invasion of Ban Hong Incident 117

Regarding the incident of British troops entering Yunnan and overstepping their authority to excavate mineral resources in Ban Hong, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has paid close attention to this. Therefore, since this problem occurred, it has advocated sending personnel to Yunnan to investigate the border areas on the one hand, and surveying and determining the border lines on the other hand. There are as many as five possible border lines in that area. After the border line problem is solved, other negotiations will be carried out.

Sino-British Trade Treaty Awaiting Negotiation 118

As for the revision of the Sino-British trade treaty and the signing of the Sino-Russian trade treaty, the reporter asked Tang. According to Tang, the revision of the Sino-British trade treaty has been rumored for a long time. Since the British envoy, Cadogan, arrived in China, the two sides have not conducted formal negotiations. Therefore, the issue of revising the Sino-British trade treaty remains to be negotiated. However, it is learned that when Wang Rutang was the Minister of Foreign Affairs, he drafted a revision draft in the department. Therefore, it is believed that the progress of this issue will take this draft as a reference. As for the signing of the Sino-Russian treaty, the two sides are now waiting to negotiate. There are many issues between China and Russia that need to be discussed, and they should be carried out one by one.

Former Turkish Prince in Shanghai 119

Regarding the current news reported by the Soviet Russian TASS that the former Turkish prince is being used by the Japanese and has gone from Shanghai to Xinjiang to plot the formation of a puppet organization, the reporter asked whether the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has received this report. According to Tang, the former Turkish prince recently came to Shanghai from Japan. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Shanghai Municipal Government are paying close attention to this. It is heard that after arriving in Shanghai, he resides in the Chinese Concession and is still in Shanghai. As to whether he will go to Xinjiang to plot a puppet organization, I have not received confirmation.

Tang Scheduled to Return to Nanjing 120

Tang is scheduled to take the night express train to Nanjing on Wednesday night to visit President Wang, and then go to Wuhan to inspect and represent President Wang to visit and comfort the mayor of Beijing, Shi Ying. He will stay for about a week and then return to Nanjing.

Huang Shaoxiong Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 121

He will return to Nanjing after staying for two or three days and then go on tour again

Central News Agency: Huang Shaoxiong, the Minister of Interior, took the night train from Nanjing the night before yesterday and arrived at the North Station at 7:30 yesterday morning. He went directly to his private residence on West Aixiensi Road to rest.
