As for the date of his tour, it will be decided after returning to Nanjing. Huang currently has no intention of going to Jiangxi. It is not true that Huang will go to Jiangxi to visit Chairman Chiang before his tour.

Overseas Chinese in Java Take the Lead in Investing in the Motherland 122

Special Envoy Mr. Lin Siwen Returns to Fujian

Investigating the Production and Sales of the Sugar Industry

In recent years, the economic panic overseas has reached its peak, and compatriots are being excluded everywhere. Therefore, the number of people investing in the motherland's industries is increasing daily. The Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Batavia, Dutch Java, held its eleventh board meeting last month. It was resolved to hire Mr. Lin Siwen to return to China and investigate the production and sales of the sugar industry in Zhangzhou, Fujian, as the precursor to overseas Chinese investing in the motherland. It is found that the amount of sugarcane sugar consumed in our country every year is very large, and the amount of sugarcane sugar imported from abroad every year is more than tens of millions of yuan, which is a major leakage. The geology and climate of the Zhangzhou area of Fujian Province are suitable for planting sugarcane and preparing for sugar production, and nearby Xiamen has convenient transportation and can be used as an export port. If large-scale factories can be used to produce sugar, the development of the national sugar industry can be controlled in the future. Newly arrived overseas Chinese now residing in Xiamen have brought back huge sums of money. According to Mr. Liu Shimu's investigation, the amount is about 70 million yuan, and they deeply feel that there is nowhere to invest. If the sugar industry develops, businesses related to other industries such as transportation can also develop accordingly, in order to fulfill the fundamental purpose of enabling people to use their talents to the fullest and land to use its resources to the fullest. This will not only be the driving force for building a new Fujian but also a shortcut for overseas Chinese to invest. Mr. Lin Siwen, originally from southern Fujian, has lived in Java, Nanyang, for generations, but he is extremely enthusiastic about advocating for the motherland's industries. He graduated from Baoding Military Academy and served as an instructor at the Whampoa Military Academy and Dean of Students at Jinan University. He is quite familiar with the situation in the country. His assignment to return to China for investigation this time is truly a fortunate choice. It is now heard that Mr. Lin will arrive in Shanghai soon and plans to go to Beijing first to visit Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee of the Executive Yuan and other agencies, requesting the government to send special commissioners to investigate together. The Ministry of Industry, the Fujian Provincial Government, and the Nanjing Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee have all received reports from the Batavia Chinese Chamber of Commerce in advance, ordering their subordinates to provide military and police protection for Mr. Lin as he travels through various places to facilitate his progress.

Fujianese Concerned About Overseas Compatriots 123

Yesterday Sent a Representative to Visit Lin Aimin

The Overseas Travel Group Rescue Association of Western Fujian, in view of the urgent crisis facing overseas Chinese, sent its chairman, Wu Yuwen, to visit Mr. Lin Aimin's residence yesterday to inquire about the situation of overseas compatriots, in order to understand the recent overseas situation. According to him, there used to be more than 200,000 overseas compatriots, who were very influential overseas. In recent years, due to the strict restrictions imposed by the local government, the number has decreased slightly. Taking Singapore as an example, in the past, nine out of ten residents there were Chinese. In recent years, the number has also decreased due to the impact of the global economic downturn. According to investigations, Singapore has a population of more than 400,000, but Chinese account for more than 300,000. However, due to various influences, overseas compatriots are in great pain. In addition, overseas Chinese in western Fujian have suffered repeated chaos in their hometowns and cannot return home, which doubles their suffering. They hope that the government and overseas compatriots will actively find ways to resettle and provide relief.

Revised Timetable for the Two Trunk Lines 124

Effective from April 1st

The revised timetable for the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo trunk lines has been completed and will be implemented from April 1st. In addition to the complete change in the running times of the 301st Ping-Shanghai and 302nd Shanghai-Ping intermodal express trains, most of the other trains on the two lines have also been slightly changed. In addition, in order to facilitate the intermodal passengers between Zhenjiang and Jiaxing stations, the 15th Zhen-Shanghai mixed regional train on the Beijing-Shanghai line is connected to the 41st Shanghai-Jiaxing mixed regional train on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line, and the 40th Jia-Shanghai mixed regional train on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line is connected to the 16th mixed regional train on the Beijing-Shanghai line. They are all operated with the same train carriages as intermodal trains between Zhenjiang and Jiaxing. Passengers do not need to change tickets or trains at Shanghai North Station. As for the train schedules of the trains on the Song-Shanghai section of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and the Yong-Cao section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, they remain unchanged according to the old schedule. The new schedule is recorded below.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's New Ships: Two to Arrive in September 129

Selecting and Sending Crew Members to England for Training

Appointing He to Drive Engine and Other Six People

Approved to Set Sail from Shanghai Next Month

Two Riverboats to Be Built by Jiangnan Shipyard

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company borrowed Sino-British Boxer Indemnity funds to build six new ships. The tenders were submitted in London. After the bureau revised the size of the ships twice, construction has now begun. The first two seagoing vessels will arrive in September this year from England to Shanghai. The bureau has sent crew members to England for training to prepare to bring the new ships to China. The shipowners and crew members have also been selected and are approved to set sail next month. The information is recorded as follows:

New Seagoing Vessels Are Being Built 130

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company borrowed 400,000 pounds of Sino-British Boxer Indemnity funds to build four new seagoing vessels in London. Special Commissioners Wu Daming and Shi Gan were sent to London to submit bids for construction. At that time, because the length of the ships did not meet the requirements and exceeded the estimated construction cost, the bureau continued to discuss and changed the length of the four new ships to 314 feet and telegraphed England to re-submit bids. As a result, a shipbuilding contract has been signed in London. A telegram has been sent to Shanghai stating that construction has begun and that the construction can be completed in about six months. The first batch of two ships will be delivered and sail to Shanghai in September this year.

Sending Personnel to England for Training 131

The bureau received a telegram stating that the ships will be delivered in September, which is not far away. Personnel should be sent to England in advance to train in the shipyard in order to understand the use of various machines and engine management technologies in the new seagoing vessels. If there is anything unclear, they can inquire in advance so that after the ships leave the factory and sail to Shanghai, they can become familiar with the situation and avoid any hindrance. After discussion, it was decided to first select six people, including drivers and engine crew, to go to England to train in the shipyard and order them to bring the ships to Shanghai.

Six Crew Members Selected 132

It has now been agreed to send two shipowners, a mechanical engineer, and four engine personnel. After investigation by the ship affairs department, the most experienced and technically superior current shipowners Ma Jiajun and Teng Shibiao were selected. Subsequently, Huang Zonglun, a mechanical engineer from the shipping department, Zhang Guoben from the Jiahe ship, and two engine specialist trainees, Li Changwen and Shi Ruichang, were selected, for a total of six people. The salaries of each employee will still be paid according to the original amount, but the round-trip travel expenses and all expenses for each person will be given at 20 to 25 pounds per month. This matter has been submitted by Liu Hongsheng to the board of directors for review.

Will Set Sail Soon 133

The bureau decided that the six people going to England will set sail from Shanghai in early April and go straight to England. It is heard that the construction of the ship is expected to be completed in about six months, and the first batch of two ships will sail to Shanghai in September this year.

Sending Personnel to England for Training 134

The bureau received a telegram stating that the ships will be delivered in September, which is not far away. Personnel should be sent to England in advance to train in the shipyard in order to understand the use of various machines and engine management technologies in the new seagoing vessels. If there is anything unclear, they can inquire in advance so that after the ships leave the factory and sail to Shanghai, they can become familiar with the situation and avoid any hindrance. After discussion, it was decided to first select six people, including drivers and engine crew, to go to England to train in the shipyard and order them to bring the ships to Shanghai.

The Price of Tap Water in the Public Concession Will Be Reduced to 80% 135

Effective from April 1st for One Year

The current tap water price in the Public Concession was agreed upon by the Public Works Department and the Water Company last year and has been in trial operation for one year since April 1st last year. At the board meeting of the Public Works Department last Wednesday, the Director General reported that the Water Company and the Water Price Review Committee had sent letters stating matters regarding water prices. The Water Price Review Committee decided on the 8th of this month to recommend to the Public Works Department that the water price be uniformly calculated at 80% from April 1st of this year, with a period of one year, and then discussed again after the expiration. The company's letter to the Public Works Department also made the same recommendation. According to the opinion of the Water Price Review Committee, the proposed discount will not affect the company's financial position, and the discount should be regarded as a temporary relief measure for users. The revision of the water price list will be discussed in detail by the committee. After discussion by the board of directors of the Public Works Department, it was decided to approve the company's request and uniformly calculate the water price at 80% from April 1st of this year.

People from all walks of life in Beijing, in view of the seriousness of the national crisis, deeply know that the promotion of national goods and the development of production cannot be delayed. The company's construction plan for national goods stipulates that cooperation in sales and production is the first step, cooperation in production and economy is the second step, and cooperation in economy and talent is the third step. Assisting various regions in establishing national goods companies is the basic work for implementing the plan. The purpose of this work is to create sales power and transform commercial organizations, gradually progressing to complete a commercial alliance. Therefore, the company attaches great importance to the establishment of the Nanjing National Goods Company. It is now heard that the company has determined to invest 10,000 yuan in the Nanjing National Goods Company and, in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the company's articles of association and the first category of organizational principles, raise 10,000 yuan in shares on its behalf. The board of directors greatly admires the company's spirit and has unanimously decided to increase the capital to 100,000 yuan. The directors present at the meeting have already subscribed to 2,000 yuan in shares, totaling 54,000 yuan. The remaining 26,000 yuan will be raised by newly appointed directors and the committee. It has been agreed that April 30 will be the deadline for collecting the funds, and Zhang Mengwen, Zhuang Xianglin, Chen Chuqiao, Huang Cilun, and Fu Zhongfu, a representative of the municipal government, will be responsible for examining the status and price of the Taiping Road Samsung Company. It is expected that the realization of the Nanjing National Goods Company will be extremely rapid. The origin of the Nanjing National Goods Company is recorded below: "The China National Goods Production and Sales Joint Company Organizes the Origin of the Nanjing National Goods Company" Today's people only know that the Great Wall bleeds blood and the Shanghai-Shanghai war is a method of defending against the enemy, but they do not know that negotiating business and starting work, protecting the economy, are also strategies for seeking strength and preparedness. When two countries compete, the enemy is strong and we are weak, the enemy exerts all its strength and we are not of one mind, then retreat is advance, and the strategy of alliance can be used as a lesson for ten years of education and training. We must endure and be able to struggle, suffer and know how to prepare, and then we can talk about revenge and save the country. This company is based on the principle of production self-rescue and engages in the construction of industrial and commercial enterprises. The reason why it engages in the construction of industrial and commercial enterprises is to expand the scope of life, resist the invasion of foreign goods, and enable the economy of the people to circulate and support themselves. If they can support themselves, they can talk about education, and then the teachings of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, and the way of self-improvement, can be widely practiced without hindrance. When this company was first established, Mayor Shi deeply knew that governing commerce was the forerunner of starting work. After implementing the movement to promote national goods, he followed up with the suggestion to establish the Nanjing National Goods Company, and the municipal government purchased 10,000 yuan in shares to encourage it. The company's responsibilities lie in complying with the municipal government's encouragement, and the first board meeting decided, in accordance with the provisions of Articles 4 and 30 of the company's articles of association, to allocate 10,000 yuan to establish the preparatory committee for organizing the Nanjing National Goods Company. It has also obtained the consent of Minister Chen and Mayor Shi to serve as the directors of the preparatory committee, leading the recruitment of shares, so that the proposal for the Nanjing National Goods Company can be realized as soon as possible, in order to conform to the true meaning of promoting national goods and meet the needs of the people to protect them. If government officials and ladies in Beijing can support them without doing small things, then not only the establishment of the Nanjing National Goods Company will be a matter of time, but also the proposal for chain stores, the transformation of commercial organizations, and the ideal of a joint industrial and commercial alliance can all be expected to be realized. This special narrative describes its origin and attaches the articles of association for raising shares, hoping for public consideration.

Innovation Plan of the Ministry of Communications 143

Merger of Wireless and Wired

Methods Are Being Drafted

According to reliable information from the communications sector, Minister of Communications Zhu Jiahua believes that wired telegraph bureaus and wireless radio stations are both state-owned electrical communications agencies and should not be separated. He has always advocated for a merger. Communications personnel also believe that the merger is a crucial plan and express their sympathy. Moreover, since postal and telecommunications have already been combined in one place, and wireless and wired have the same nature, it is even more inappropriate to separate and govern separately. Therefore, in order to realize the new plan of merging wireless and wired as soon as possible, the Electrical Affairs Department of the Ministry is actively drafting regulations, and the department in charge of electrical affairs has sent circulars to the responsible personnel of telegraph bureaus and wireless radio stations in various places, instructing them to immediately submit their opinions on the implementation methods for reference.

Japanese Merchants Lower Prices to Attract Chinese Merchants, the Customs Declaration Industry Is Severely Hit 144

Difficult to Profit, Cancel the Car Force Competition

Workers Oppose and Will Use Strikes to Deal With It

According to Xin Sheng She, the Chinese customs declaration industry has been severely affected by the establishment of customs declaration firms by Japanese merchants in Shanghai and the reduction of freight rates to attract business. The customs declaration firms of the Tianjin gang have canceled the car force, which has aroused the workers' reaction. The details are recorded below:

Customs Declaration by Japanese Merchants 145

Customs declaration workers once experienced a strike due to the cancellation of the traditional cartage fees by various cotton fabric businesses. Fortunately, the strike was resolved after mediation by party and government authorities, and the cartage fees were handled as usual. Now, it is reported that Chinese-owned customs brokerages in the Tianjin business community are suffering because Japanese merchants have established customs brokerages in Shanghai, such as Pingqia, to solicit customs declarations and disrupt the established cartage fee practices. Initially, they only handled Japanese goods, but now they are arbitrarily reducing fees and soliciting packaging business. Merchants from various Tianjin business groups are taking advantage of their low prices and using their services, significantly impacting the business of Chinese customs brokerages.

Price War 146

Chinese customs brokerages are struggling to profit due to the competitive impact of the Japanese customs brokerages. To maintain their operations, they will also reduce freight charges and abolish cartage fees starting this year to compete with Japanese merchants. The first to implement this is Yufengsheng Customs Brokerage, and other firms such as Fuji are following suit. The profit margin per item has become very small.

Workers' Opposition 147

Customs declaration workers from the Tianjin business community oppose the Tianjin business community and customs brokerages for disrupting established practices and abolishing cartage fees, which has severely impacted their livelihoods. They have collectively protested and petitioned the Municipal Party Department's Social Affairs Bureau for assistance. They are also holding meetings to discuss countermeasures and, if necessary, will resort to strikes against customs brokerages that disrupt the cartage fee system. The Social Affairs Bureau has already begun mediation, and the Customs Brokerage Association will hold a general meeting in the coming days to discuss the matter.

Dumping in North China 148

Japanese goods, such as cotton yarn, cotton cloth, and general merchandise, have experienced a significant decrease in sales in various parts of South China due to the boycott by the Chinese people. However, they are still being sold as usual in various parts of North China. According to sources in the customs declaration industry, eight or nine out of ten goods handled by merchants from the Tianjin business community are Japanese goods. It is reported that in recent days, North China steamships transporting Japanese goods to Tianjin and other places have been carrying two to three thousand items daily, mostly on Japanese ships.

Muslims' Grand Prayer Yesterday Morning 155

For Muslims, performing the Hajj (pilgrimage to Mecca) is the highest honor. Those who cannot personally perform the Hajj must perform ablutions and prayers in local mosques on the seventieth day after Ramadan each year, which is traditionally called the Lesser Eid. Yesterday morning, at ten mosques in Shanghai, Muslims gathered to perform ablutions and change clothes. At 9:30 AM, they prayed devoutly and then personally performed Qurbani (sacrificing livestock such as cattle, sheep, chickens, and ducks), giving gifts to relatives and friends in the community and donating to the poor Muslims. It is said that Muslims around the world perform this same grand ritual.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter to Municipal Council Regarding Agency for Land Goods Industry Donation and License Fees 156

And Requests that the Fee Remains at Two Dollars per Quarter

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Municipal Council yesterday stating, "To whom it may concern, on the 24th of this month, we received a letter from our member Land Goods Industry Association stating that the council had previously forced members of their industry to donate to obtain licenses. After repeated negotiations, the council replied that it was not convenient to approve the exemption from the donation, but the license fee was reduced to two dollars per quarter, as stated in your council's letter No. 345 of the Puzi series of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Now, the Municipal Council has sent personnel to collect the license fee from various firms in the industry, increasing the fee by four dollars per license without explaining the reason for the increase. The personnel of various firms in our association, not being literate in foreign languages, assumed that the fee was calculated on a semi-annual basis, so they all paid the fee. Later, they learned that it was a quarterly donation fee, and they have petitioned the association to negotiate with the Municipal Council to continue collecting the fee at the original amount. We have found that the Municipal Council's change to the previously determined donation amount and its sudden collection from various firms in the industry seems to be a breach of contract. To avoid disputes, our association will not retroactively recover the increased license fee for the previous quarter. Starting this summer, the fee will be paid at the original amount. We are afraid that there will be further increases in the future. It is now proposed that the quarterly license fee to be paid by various firms in the industry should be collected by our association, and we request that your council forward it to the Municipal Council, and the council should issue licenses for each firm to our association for distribution. We respectfully request that the council not increase the fee, so as to comply with the original plan and avoid disputes. We would be deeply grateful. Enclosed is a list of the names of various firms donating licenses and seventy-two dollars for the summer donation of licenses. We are sending this letter to request that you forward it to the Municipal Council and ask the council to instruct the donation office to count the money and issue the licenses. This is our sincere request. Furthermore, due to preliminary issues in this session, we are directly negotiating with your council. Once the two proposed methods of the association have been negotiated and agreed upon, our association can directly send a letter to the donation office regarding future license matters."

Sichuan Survey Group of the Engineering Society to Depart on Schedule 157

丨Departing from Shanghai on April 15th丨

The sole purpose of this trip is to seek the welfare of Sichuan

Working in groups to conduct thorough investigations and research

Liu Fucheng (Xiang), the Military Governor of Sichuan, has repeatedly thwarted bandit forces since his command to suppress the Sichuan bandits, and success is expected soon. In order to develop production and construction, he telegraphed the Shanghai Chinese Engineering Society last year to conduct a survey in Sichuan. The society believed that Sichuan and Tibet were rich in resources and urgently needed to be surveyed in order to develop them. They immediately carefully hired specialists and organized the Sichuan Survey Group. Fortunately, with the sincere cooperation of all parties, preparations are nearing completion, and it has been decided that they will depart on April 15th. Hu Shuhua, the President of Hunan University in Changsha, will serve as the head of the group.

Details are pre-announced as follows:

Purpose of Departure 158

The Chinese Engineering Society, in view of the upcoming departure of the survey group, has specially notified each group member of the purpose of the departure, the work to be undertaken, and the matters related to the group members' travel expenses. (1) Purpose of Departure: Although some members of this group serve in government agencies, this trip is purely to fulfill their national duty and contribute their knowledge and experience to seek the welfare of China and Sichuan. There is absolutely no other political meaning or effect. The members of this group do not represent the agencies to which they belong. Although some members of this group come from the industrial and commercial sectors, the purpose of this trip is not to promote their private business or sell their goods. Developing Sichuan is a way to save the country. Although people from other provinces can participate in Sichuan's undertakings, due to geographical relations, Sichuan should still be the main entity. People from other provinces are only willing to play a supporting role. The central government and local governments should cooperate closely, but the central government will never compete with local governments for power and profit. Our society is an academic organization and only knows how to serve, and has no rights to speak of. The above three points can be explained at any time in Sichuan to avoid misunderstandings.

Group Work 159

After arriving in Chongqing or Chengdu, the members of each group will work in groups. Their itineraries will not interfere with each other, but they must report to the head of the group, who will schedule the itinerary for each group. The members of each group should collect materials in advance for the issues they are responsible for. After entering Sichuan, they should quickly contact and liaise with the local person in charge, inquire about the difficulties, and conduct thorough investigations and research. If there are proposals, they must be carefully discussed at the group meeting before they are submitted. Do not act alone. If a decision cannot be made, it is okay to say so directly, and it is not appropriate to be perfunctory. The head of this group was originally Mr. Sa Fujun, the president of the society. Because President Sa is traveling to the Americas, Director Hu Shuhua has been recommended to take over. The representative of the Sichuan side who is in charge of all the affairs of the survey group is Mr. Gan Diankui, the Director of Political Affairs (stationed in Chongqing).

Group Members' Travel Expenses 160

The departure from China is scheduled for April 14th or 15th, departing from Shanghai. Nanjing and Hankou can also stop to pick up members of the group who are boarding in Beijing and Hankou. The exact date and name of the ship will be notified later. The average travel expenses for each member of the group (one person is already in Sichuan) are estimated at 1,000 yuan, all of which will be borne by the Sichuan Post-Disaster Rehabilitation Office. Extra travel expenses for those departing from places other than Beijing, Hankou, and Shanghai can also be included in the calculation. The accounting affairs will be handled by a specialist appointed by the Bank of China commissioned by the office and will be under the command of the head of the group. (For the members' personal use, Sichuan Representative Fan Chongshi stationed in Beijing has been asked to send some money to each person when boarding the ship for emergencies, but each person should still bring some pocket money.) This trip to Sichuan is not for sightseeing.

Therefore, it is advisable not to bring family members.

Liaison Matters 161

Assistants needed for investigation, survey, or measurement can be obtained by discussing with Political Affairs Director Gan Diankui and Loo Sak-fu, General Manager of Minsheng Industrial Company after arriving in Chongqing. All other issues can also be discussed with these two gentlemen. The China Western Academy of Sciences in Beibei, Chengdu University, and West China University can all provide research materials. Travel light for the spring season, but bedding must be brought. Servants do not need to be brought in order to maintain uniformity. The weather in inland Sichuan is warmer and the scenery is beautiful, so travelers will feel happy. The opium scourge in Sichuan is pervasive and deeply rooted, which is very sad. The group can take the opportunity to express their concerns to the authorities. Mr. Zhang Yujiu of the Bank of China in Sichuan is a man of heart, and his Sichuan Monthly magazine is worth noting. The magazine is available on the ship, so please read it. After arriving in Shanghai, members of the group can contact Mr. Zhang Shulin, Shanghai Manager of Minsheng Company at No. 16, O-zi, Jiujiang Road. Mr. Zhang has also decided to accompany them to Sichuan, so they can take care of each other along the way. Members of the group who are boarding the ship in Hankou must arrive in Hankou on April 15th and inquire about everything from Mr. Li Longzhang of Minsheng Branch Company at No. 2, Dingan Lane. If members of the group have any questions before boarding the ship, please contact Yun Zhen of the Construction Committee.

Standard for Passengers Kidnapped on the Yisheng Wheel 163

Those with fair and tender arms and wrinkle-free feet

Are Considered by Bandits to be Wealthy and Honored

Even the Poor Are Considered Rich

The Yisheng Wheel is Expected to Arrive in Shanghai Today

The Yisheng Wheel of Jardine Matheson was hijacked on the 12th of this month in the waters off Fuzhou, and six passengers were taken away. The ship is expected to arrive in Shanghai today. The details heard are supplemented as follows:

Hell Money Attracts Covetous Pirates 164

The hijacking of the Yisheng Wheel was caused by three boxes of hell money loaded on the ship. The pirates mistook the hell money for real currency, so when the 22 pirates took action on the 12th, they asked the crew for the money. The crew told them that what was loaded was hell money, not silver coins, but the bandits had already taken action and searched all the passengers on the ship.

Twenty-Two Pirates with Seven Guns 165

The pirates who hijacked the Yisheng Wheel spoke with a complete Huizhou accent. There were a total of twenty-two people, and they only brought seven guns on board. They searched the ship for a total of sixteen or seventeen hours, and the total amount of cash they looted, including from the crew and passengers, was only about 5,000 yuan. Each pirate received about 200 yuan, but some received two shares and some only received half a share, depending on their status among the bandits. Because there was not much cash, they kidnapped passengers.

No News of Six Hostages 166

At that time, the bandits detained 17 passengers on the ship for them to choose to kidnap. The bandits kidnapped passengers based on their clothes and limbs. Those with fair arms and wrinkle-free feet were considered to be wealthy and honored people. Six people were taken away on the spot, including two passengers surnamed Pan from Nanjing, one passenger each surnamed Cheng and Chen, and two others, Zhang Boyu, a shop assistant from the Huashangtai Company, and Zhang Xiting, who had been unemployed for more than ten years. They were all poor people with no family wealth, and their whereabouts are still unknown.

Lu Xuefang's Quick Wit 167

When comprador Lu Xuefang heard of the robbery at 5:00 AM on the 12th, he disguised himself as a stoker and walked out of the cabin door. He met a bandit who wanted to go to the captain's room but did not know the way. Lu falsely agreed to lead him to a ladder, and then took the opportunity to escape into the coal bunker. He hid in the coal for 36 hours. The bandit leader searched for Lu everywhere and offered a reward of 300 yuan for Lu on the ship. Fortunately, a teaboy told the bandits that Lu had jumped into the sea and drowned. The bandits finally gave up. With his quick wit, Lu was not kidnapped.

Xu's Case Dismissed on Appeal 168

Xu Yuying Petitions for Restoration

The Second Branch of the High Court Dismisses the Request

In the case of Ji Juemi, the chief manager of Hadong, being sued for seducing Xu Yuying, a young girl from Ningbo, after the first instance trial by the First Special District District Court, Ji Juemi was found not guilty. The plaintiffs, Xu Li Shi and Xu Yuying, were unwilling to accept the verdict and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. When the court scheduled the trial for the afternoon of the 20th of last month, the appellant did not appear because she had applied to the Supreme Court for a transfer of jurisdiction. Subsequently, her application was rejected by the Supreme Court. The Second Branch of the High Court then set the afternoon of March 12th as the date for the retrial and ordered the police to summon them to Xu's mother and daughter's residence at No. 13, Daodali Road, Beile Road, in the French Concession. However, they still did not appear on the scheduled date. On the one hand, they petitioned for a postponement of the trial on the grounds that Xu Yuying was ill, so the court could not be opened again that day. Later, after the criminal court president Yu Hua and the jurors Zhao Zheng Tang, Zhou Han, and Jiang presented it for review, they believed that the appellant was deliberately delaying the case. The lawsuit had been legally served, but they still repeatedly avoided interrogation. Therefore, on the 17th of this month, they ruled to dismiss the appeal and posted the ruling on the court's notice board, as Xu's residence address in the petition was No. 13, Daodali Road, Beile Road, but the summons and other documents sent there were not received. After the announcement, Xu Li Shi and Xu Yuying submitted a petition to the Second Branch of the High Court, requesting the revocation of the ruling to "dismiss the appeal" and the restoration of the case. After Judge Yu and jurors Zhao and Zhou considered the matter, they found that their request had no merit and rejected it on the 24th. The Ji Xu lawsuit, which had been widely publicized and attracted attention throughout the city, now seems to be coming to an end.

Major Disturbance in District Four Over Crackdown on Vegetable Stalls on Jingjiang Road 169

District Officials and Stallholders Injured in Clashes

Shops on Gonghe Xin Road Go on Strike

Yesterday morning, the Zhongxing Road Police Station of the Public Security Bureau of District Four of Zhabei dispatched police to crack down on vegetable stalls along Jingjiang Road and arrested ten people. Stallholders went to the police station to petition, causing a disturbance. District official Ouyang Liu was injured in the clash, and some stallholders were also injured. The details are as follows:

History of the Stalls 170

In the area north of the railway on Gonghe Xin Road, Zhabei, there have long been poor people from Jiangbei setting up vegetable stalls to earn a meager income to make a living. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, Yang Dexing petitioned the municipal government to organize the Daxing Company to purchase land and build a cement vegetable market at the intersection of Zhongxing Road, charging each stallholder six jiao. For a time, the stalls were quite crowded. Subsequently, the fees continued to increase to two yuan, so many stallholders were unable to pay. They then set up stalls on the wasteland along Jingjiang Road, and the stallholders in the vegetable market became increasingly scarce, and business was very slow. They then petitioned the Public Security Bureau to crack down on hawkers along the road and force them to move in, but most stallholders, having survived the war and the great fire after the war, were unable to pay the donation, so they refused to return to the vegetable market.

Dispatching Police to Crack Down 171

Lai Gang, the Director of the Public Security Bureau of District Four, believed that the stalls along the road violated police regulations and ordered district official Ouyang Liu of the Zhongxing Road Police Station to dispatch police to drive them away. On the 17th of this month, he arrested nine stallholders and sent them to the General Public Security Bureau for interrogation. As a result, five people were sentenced to imprisonment and were released a few days ago. At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, the district official dispatched more than ten policemen to Jingjiang Road to drive away all the stallholders, but the stallholders refused to obey, resulting in a conflict. The police then detained ten of the ringleaders and took them back to the police station for detention.

Disturbance Occurs 172

The stallholders were panicked by the police station's arrest of ten stallholders. They gathered three or four hundred stallholders, old and young, and went to the Zhongxing Road District Four Police Station to petition, demanding immediate release, otherwise they would not leave. For a time, a conflict occurred due to misinterpretation of words. Some people threw stones, smashing the windows and glass of the police station, and the order was quite chaotic. The police chief, seeing the situation, dispatched police to drive them away, but to no avail. He also called the Director of the Public Security Bureau of District Four for instructions. Lai Gang, upon hearing the news, immediately led more than 20 policemen to suppress the situation, but the crowd still did not disperse. He then telegraphed the General Public Security Bureau to dispatch more than 20 machine gun team members to assist in the dispersal, which was successful.

Persuading to Open the Market 173

The shops along Gonghe Xin Road from the railway north to Zhongxing Road, seeing this situation, went on strike around 11:00 AM at noon. In the afternoon, Lai Gang, the District Chief of District Four, personally led the police to persuade each household to open the market. Although a small number of shops opened for business in the evening, most were still closed.

Injured Police and Civilians 174

Afterwards, reporters rushed to investigate the injuries of police and civilians. The situation is as follows: Ouyang Liu, a Fourth District officer, suffered severe injuries to his waist, a broken nose and bleeding, and a black eye. He was taken to the Bao Long Hospital for treatment. Police officers Chen Huamin, Zhou Qingjun, Fan Caisheng, Cai Chongting, Zhu Lizhao, and others were also injured and sent to the Second Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society for treatment. On the side of the stallholders, the injured included Madam Yang, 54 years old, from Jiangbei, and Madam Li Xu, 79 years old, two elderly people from Jiangbei, who both had head injuries and were sent to the Red Cross by the Fourth District Public Security Bureau. Zhu Nianhui, 29 years old, from Jiangbei, suffered a head injury. Others such as Madam Zhang Song, 55 years old, Madam Qin Zhao, 51 years old, Madam Yang Yao, 57 years old, and Madam Zhu Lou, 24 years old, suffered minor injuries.

Ten People Sent to the Bureau 175

Furthermore, the ten stall vendors initially detained, namely Zhang Guyu, Zhang Rongfu, Madam Zhou Song, Yang Yao, Madam Xing Cao, Zhu Lianyuan, Madam Zhu Xu, Chen Shuicai, Li Xu, and Madam Zhu Yang, were sent to the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau by the Fourth District yesterday afternoon for interrogation.

Rushing to Investigate 176

The Municipal Party Headquarters, upon receiving a report that shops along Gonghe Xin Road in Zhabei had gone on strike, requested prompt action. After receiving the report, the headquarters immediately dispatched Investigation Section Director Zhang Yunzeng, General Manager Lu Yuanhu, together with Civil Affairs Section General Manager Zhang Sheng, Secretary Lu Yinchu, and others to rush to investigate the truth in order to assist in handling the situation. Furthermore, the Public Security Bureau also dispatched an Inspector-General and police officers yesterday to rush to investigate and ensure fair handling of the matter.

Reporting the Incident 177

The Zhongxing Road Police Station, after the incident, immediately submitted a written report to the Fourth District, which was forwarded to the Municipal Government Public Security Bureau. The original text reads: Regarding the matter of reporting, at 8:30 AM today, Police Chief Li of the Machine Gun Squad led police officers to crack down on vegetable stalls on Jingjiang Road. The stall vendors not only refused to comply with the crackdown but also injured police officers Chen Jimin, Zhou Qingjun, Fan Caisheng, Cai Chongting, and Zhu Lizhao. Upon seeing the injured officers, Police Chief Li immediately arrested the ringleaders Zhang Jinzhen, Zhu Lianyuan, Zhang Chengfu, and others, and took them to the station. When they arrived at the intersection of Gonghe Xin Road and Zhongxing Road, several hundred vegetable stallholders seized one shell gun from police officer Chen Jimin. The gun was later recovered with the assistance of soldiers from the Second Squad of the Security Team, but the gun belt was torn. When I heard the news and was about to dispatch more police officers to maintain order, three or four hundred people suddenly arrived and surrounded the police station, destroying all the furniture, doors, windows, bedding, office equipment, and other items inside. They then grabbed and beat me, tearing my uniform and causing me serious injuries. Then, they dragged me away. When we reached Datong Road and Zhongxing Road, fortunately, the district patrol arrived and rescued me. I found that several police officers from the gun squad had been injured and immediately sent them to the Second Hospital of the Red Cross for treatment. Several police officers at the station suffered minor injuries, and cook Hu Jinshan injured his leg. Most of the uniforms were torn, and two Russian-made gun mechanisms, two rubber raincoats, and one Bailinglin gun were snatched away. 46 yuan in silver dollars and one gold watch that I carried with me were also snatched away. The police station is currently investigating the items lost by the station chief. After a detailed investigation, I will report again. Respectfully submitted.

Detailed Account of Westerner Julian's Suicide 178

Girlfriend Unsuccessful in Suicide Attempt After Taking Poison Last Night

His Life Story Was Truly Remarkable

Last week, a suicide case occurred at the Astor House Hotel on the Bund. A foreigner claiming to be a British Canadian named (C.C. Julian) Cecil Julian died after taking poison. In addition, his girlfriend (Leonora.Levy) Leonora Levy also attempted suicide by taking poison, but fortunately, she was rescued and her life was saved. It has been found that Julian was wanted by the US government and had not yet been brought to justice. The crimes he committed during his lifetime were quite shocking. The findings of the investigation are recorded as follows:

Julian and Levy's Backgrounds 179

Julian was a British Canadian. His origin was in Willow Creek, Canada. He came to Shanghai in March of last year. Julian's business in the United States had failed. After being sued and arrested in court, he seized the opportunity of being released on bail and secretly came to Shanghai. Julian was 48 years old. He had a wife, two daughters, and a brother named Cecil Julian in his hometown. His brother was also recently sued in the United States, but was ultimately granted probation. Julian's business in the United States was enormous. He served as the president of the Julian Petroleum Corporation. The company's capital reached 100 million, but the result was that the oil mining yielded no results. As a result, the company declared bankruptcy, and Julian was sued by many people, accused of being a huge swindler. Therefore, his past history was well-known to people throughout the United States. As for Ms. Levy, who did not succeed in committing suicide, she was a close friend of Julian. It was rumored that she was Julian's secretary, which has been denied. Ms. Levy had been living in Shanghai. Her father, Gotonberg, was in the film business in Shanghai. However, in 1925, he was murdered in the Victoria Theatre. Her mother was British and remarried soon after. Levy took her stepfather's surname and was only nineteen years old. She was a beautiful and charming young woman.

Julian Commits Suicide First, Then the Girl Takes Poison 180

Julian's suicide occurred at about 9:00 PM on Saturday of last week, in room 300 of the Astor House Hotel where Julian resided. At about 8:00 PM that evening, Julian and Levy came in together from outside, looking very tired. The waiter served them dinner, but Julian did not eat. At about 9:00 PM, a woman's crying was suddenly heard in the room. The waiter entered and learned that Julian had committed suicide by taking poison. He was rushed to a doctor for treatment and sent by car to Hong En Hospital on Great Western Road. However, he had taken too much poison and died at 1:00 AM. Ms. Levy also went with him at the time. Seeing this situation, she left the hospital and went to the residence of David Baker on Avenue Joffre to rest. At 6:30 AM, she went out. At 9:15 AM, Levy suddenly collapsed while borrowing a telephone at a pharmacy at No. 1703 Jing'an Temple Road, unconscious. She was sent to Hong En Hospital by car. A bottle of Amytal pills was found next to her, indicating that she had also taken poison. She was given treatment, and fortunately, the amount of poison was small. She gradually regained consciousness, and her life is now safe. However, she is still very weak, so she is still being treated at Hong En Hospital.

The Deceased Shook the Entire United States During His Lifetime 181

Julian, who committed suicide, was initially a clothing salesman. Because he was talented, he later suddenly engaged in the oil mining business. Although he failed several times, he was able to rise again by virtue of his eloquence. Years ago, he reorganized the Julian Petroleum Corporation. The initial capital was only 30 million, but he gradually increased it to 100 million through publicity methods. Unexpectedly, the oil mines dug in the western United States yielded no results, so he declared bankruptcy. More than 15,000 people were affected. As a result, many people sued Julian. The court in Ardmore, Oklahoma, also charged Julian with two counts of fraud and embezzlement and arrested him. However, he was released on bail of $25,000. Julian seized this opportunity to escape from Ardmore to Vancouver, and from Vancouver to Shanghai. At that time, the US authorities offered a reward of $3,000 for his arrest. However, because Julian claimed to be Canadian and was under British protection, the US consulate in Shanghai intended to extradite him, but failed due to the opposition of the British consulate.

Using the Hotel as Home Due to Knowing Levy 182

When Julian first came to Shanghai, he stayed at the Palace Hotel. At the end of last year, he moved into the Cathay Hotel on the Bund. But two weeks later, he moved to a Western apartment on Carter Road. At that time, his bedroom was next to Ms. Levy's, so they got to know each other. Julian was very down on his luck in Shanghai, but he once worked as the general manager of a stock brokerage firm on the Continental Building. Ms. Levy also worked there. However, Julian suddenly resigned in early February of this year, and Ms. Levy also left her job. Two days before the suicide, Julian suddenly moved to room 300 of the Astor House Hotel. Ms. Levy, on the other hand, moved to the David's Hotel on Saturday of last week, which was also reserved by Julian in advance. It is said that Levy had just arrived from Hankou. Who knew that this tragedy would happen that evening?

Speculation About the Cause of Death is Widespread 183

There are various rumors about Julian's suicide. Some say that because the US president recently approved an important bill, all American fugitives, if their place of residence is in an area where the US government enjoys extraterritorial rights, can be extradited. Therefore, Julian would have no foothold in Shanghai, so he committed suicide. Others say that Julian's business failure was certain, and he did not bring much capital with him when he came to Shanghai. Recently, he had been in dire straits. He had attempted suicide once two weeks ago, but was discovered by a friend and failed. Recently, he had shown signs of pessimism and had written a special autobiography, saying that when people reach the end of their road, they begin to understand the psychology of those who commit suicide. His desire to commit suicide did not start today. As for Ms. Levy's suicide, it was due to her emotional connection with Julian.

The Authorities Begin to Investigate 184

Since the case has been started being investigated by the British Assessor's Office in this port. After Julian's body was sent to the morgue on Fearon Road, British Coroner Maurice went to examine it and held a preliminary hearing. The hearing was adjourned until 2:00 PM this Thursday. The only person related to the case is Ms. Levy. The British authorities originally intended to question her, but because Ms. Levy's health had not recovered, they decided to postpone it. The authorities have also begun investigating Julian's estate. According to the investigation, he has nothing, so Julian's suicide is also greatly related to economic problems. (Huadong News Agency)

Robbery and Killing on Min Ti Ni Yin Road One Thief Shot and Killed 185

The Thief Fired Four Shots, None of Which Hit

The Thief's Corpse Lies in a Busy Street, His Death is Very Tragic

At 7:01 PM last night, a robbery occurred on Min Ti Ni Yin Road, north of the Chu Family Bridge, in the French Concession. The victim followed the thieves closely in pursuit. Multiple Chinese and Vietnamese constables along the way, as well as Chinese constables on duty in the Chinese district, surrounded and arrested the thieves from all sides. The robbers opened fire to resist arrest, and as a result, one thief was shot and killed on the spot. The details are as follows:

Four Thieves Break In 186

Xu Zhishan, from Yangzhou, specializes in buying old stamps. He married a woman named He and rented a residence at No. 31, Lane 7, Jin Yu Li, north of the Chu Family Bridge on Min Ti Ni Yin Road in the French Concession. At 7:01 PM last night, Xu had just finished his work and returned home, preparing to have dinner, when suddenly four robbers broke in from outside the door. One thief stood guard outside the door, while three thieves rushed in, took out pistols, and threatened them to remain silent.

Secretly Following 187

After entering the house, the robbers went into the hall and rooms to search as they pleased, and locked Xu and He in a room. As a result, they robbed a gemstone ring, a gold bracelet, and 16 yuan in cash. After obtaining the loot, the robbers fled in a hurry. At that time, Xu witnessed the robbers all escaping together, so he mustered his courage and followed them secretly. The thieves turned south then east, from Rue P. Henry straight into the Chinese district's Xiaobeimen and up to Wanzhu Street.

Four Shots Miss 188

When Xu reached Wanzhu Street, he secretly reported the crime to Constable No. 1309 from the First Section of the Second District Police Station, who assisted in the pursuit. When they reached Qinglian Street, one of the thieves noticed them and quickly turned around to open fire to resist arrest, firing four shots in succession. Fortunately, none of them hit. The constable, because there were many passersby, was afraid of injuring the innocent, so he did not return fire. Seeing that the situation was not good, the thief fled across the Chinese district's Minguo Road from Dajing Street and then back into the French Concession's Milu Road.

Bullet Hits the Thief Leader 189

At that time, police whistles sounded everywhere. Two Vietnamese constables, Nos. 260 and 466, and Chinese constable No. 601, happened to be on duty there. Hearing the alarm, they all came to meet and pursue the thief. The thief desperately rushed past the three constables, turned north at the Nanyang Bridge iron gate, and re-entered Min Ti Min Yin Road. The three constables then raised their guns together and concentrated their fire on the thief. Chinese constable No. 601 fired two shots in succession, neither of which hit. Finally, Vietnamese constable No. 260 shot the thief in the head with a rifle.

Killed on the Spot 190

The thief was hit by the bullet and immediately fell at the entrance of the Shengda Wood Company at No. 391. The three constables rushed forward together and captured him, but they saw that the bullet had entered from the back of his head and pierced his mouth, with his brains splattered. He was already dead. A live pistol containing three bullets was abandoned on the ground. The thief was wearing a light blue Chinese silk cotton robe and rubber running shoes. At the same time, the police had heard the news and dispatched a large number of detectives to the scene. They carried the thief's body into the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall to prepare the corpse for examination at the Second Special Court today.

Fire on East Broadway Road Burns Nine People to Death 191

Three More People Injured by the Fire

All are Being Treated in the Hospital

At around 10:00 PM the night before last, a fire suddenly broke out at No. 344 Xingqing Li, East Broadway Road. The fire was very fierce and spread to Nos. 343 and 345. All three buildings were completely destroyed. The fire also affected the upper floors of Nos. 346 and 347 and burned to death as many as nine people, including men, women, and children. These included Tang Ahua, a male, 31 years old; Wu Ruizhang, 3 years old; and three boys, all only four months old. The women included Tang Xing Wenxiang, 28 years old; Xin Zhou, 52 years old; Shi Zhaodi, 10 years old; Wu Wang, 20 years old; Lu Juqing, 3 years old; and Zhang Amao, 8 years old. Later, the fire brigade drove to the scene to put out the fire and tried to remove the corpses. Together with the Hongkou Police Station in charge, they ordered detectives to send the nine corpses to the morgue on Fearon Road. The facts were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Local Court dispatched Prosecutor Guo Wei, together with two forensic doctors Wei and Zhang, and court clerk Wang Zuyi, to the morgue to examine the bodies. It was determined that all of them had been burned to death before death. The families were notified to collect the coffins separately. It is heard that there are also three men and women who were burned in the fire and are currently being treated in the hospital.

Mr. Yan Shuzhai Passes Away 192

Mr. Yan Shuzhai, secretary of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and Deputy Section Chief of the First Section, has served in the Public Security Bureau for more than twenty years. He has been just, diligent, and cautious, and has always been valued by his superiors. His relationship with all sectors of society has also been extremely harmonious. Due to overwork, he passed away suddenly at 8:00 PM yesterday (the 26th). The funeral will be held at the hour of Wei on the 29th. All who heard the news were saddened.

Page 12

Murder Case Over Five Yuan Rent Results in Sentencing 193

Li Zhongxian Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

Rong Laosan, a man from Menghe, lived in the overhanging building in the redwood workshop opened by Chen Yonglin on Zijin Street in the city. Because land in Shanghai is expensive, he tried to save rent, so he built a mezzanine in this small room and rented it to Li Zhongxian, a Shandong man who sold pancakes, for five yuan a month. However, because Li owed rent and did not pay it, and Rong was unwilling to suffer losses, they had a quarrel in the early morning of the day of the incident. When Li returned home in the evening, Rong was already asleep. Li went to the mezzanine and drank alone, and when he thought of the events of the day, he cursed loudly. Rong responded from the bed, and they exchanged insults. Li became even more angry and grabbed a sharp knife, climbed down from the mezzanine, and carried out the murder. At that time, Rong was sitting on the edge of the bed, holding his child and letting him urinate, because the child had woken him up. Li Zhongxian kicked open the door and rushed in. Rong saw him and quickly put down the child and tried to escape, but Li's knife had already pierced Rong's chest, hitting the Xuehai point below the nipple. After being injured, he immediately collapsed and died. Rong's wife stepped forward to stop him and was also stabbed in the finger. Li was about to flee when the owner of the redwood workshop called the police, who arrested Li and sent him to the Public Security Bureau, which transferred him to the Local Court. Li confessed to the murder, so the presiding judge reviewed the circumstances and found that the defendant had committed murder over a trivial matter and was extremely malicious. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, Li Zhongxian was brought to court and sentenced to life imprisonment and deprivation of political rights to serve as a warning.

Investigation of the House Collapse Case at Dayang Bridge Yesterday 194

The fact that five people were killed or injured in the house collapse at the Zhongxing Huayi Factory on Zhongxing Road in Zhabei the night before last has been reported in the newspapers. Now it is learned that Li Qingjie, a patrol officer from the Taiyangmiao Police Station of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau, led Police Chief Yang Jintang, Zhao Fangwen, and others yesterday morning to investigate and found that one of the deceased was Jin Taishan, and the other was Jin's wife, Pu, who had two daughters and one son. Except for the two daughters, who were injured and sent to the hospital, the son, who was about sixteen or seventeen years old, has not been found after repeated summons. Another deceased, Cai Bugao, had a son and daughter-in-law. The son was in Wusong, and his daughter-in-law went to Wusong to find her husband and has not returned. The cause of the house collapse was that there were many Jiangbei shacks behind the factory buildings, and most of the residents raised pigs. The shacks where Jin and Cai lived were close to the eaves of the factory building. A culvert, about a foot wide and four or five zhang long, was dug under the wall. After years of water accumulation, the soil loosened, causing the disaster. Yesterday at 3:00 PM, the Local Court dispatched Prosecutor Xiao Jinying to the scene to examine the bodies. It was determined that they had been crushed to death before death. He ordered the families of the deceased to collect the bodies for burial on their own. If the families of the deceased refused to collect the bodies, the head of the Baojia would collect them for burial. It is also learned that the construction cost of the factory building was 1,200 yuan.

Special Commissioner Mei Shuzeng Departs for Sichuan to Investigate Industrial Construction 195

The Executive Yuan recently appointed Mr. Mei Shuzeng as a special commissioner to investigate industrial construction in Sichuan. After receiving the order, Mr. Mei believed that Sichuan has a vast land and abundant resources, and there are countless industries that need to be developed urgently, especially wool textiles, which are currently the most urgent need. Therefore, he went to North China to investigate the organization of wool textile factories in Tianjin and other places. He returned to Shanghai three days ago and is scheduled to go to Beijing last night, take a boat to Hankou, and then take a plane to Sichuan. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Mei at his residence yesterday. The following is a transcript of Mr. Mei's remarks: "Since I was appointed to investigate industrial construction in Sichuan, I have deeply felt that the mission is very important. Sichuan has always been known as the 'Land of Abundance,' with abundant resources and a large population. Its products supply many to the entire country, and the consumption of the people is also large. In terms of industrial construction, the future holds endless hope. Sichuan produces a lot of wool, and the quality is also good. At present, in addition to cotton and silk fabrics, the demand for wool fabrics is gradually increasing. I have long had the intention of establishing a wool textile industry in Sichuan. Therefore, when I was in Shanghai, I repeatedly visited wool textile factories such as Huazhang. This time, I was ordered to make another trip to North China to visit various wool textile factories in the north to prepare for the establishment of a wool textile enterprise in Sichuan. As for other products in Sichuan, they are too numerous to mention, such as medicinal materials, tung oil, silk, and sugar, all of which are very large. In the past, Sichuan's imports and exports often had a surplus, but since 19, a deficit has gradually appeared. At present, the annual deficit is about 10 million yuan or more. This is due to the national and even the world's economic decline, but it is also inexcusable that the responsibility of personnel has not been fully organized. In the past, Sichuan was often troubled, and there was no talk of developing any industry. Recently, Chairman Liu unified the military and government, and worked hard to govern. With this excellent opportunity, starting to develop industries should not be delayed any longer. Moreover, in the wake of our country's weakness and foreign insults, to strengthen ourselves, we must revitalize industry. The most promising place is Sichuan. Sichuan is Sichuan for the whole of China. Developing Sichuan's industry is the foundation for revitalizing China. However, relying solely on the strength of the people of Sichuan is certainly not enough. What I hope for is that the national economic community, in view of the need to develop Sichuan's industry, will rise up and work together to achieve great results. Many industrialists from other provinces do not understand the situation in Sichuan and are often hesitant. Now, these ideas are gradually changing. The news community's investigation group went to Sichuan first, followed by the engineers' investigation group. These two groups, standing as third parties, should be able to see the truth of Sichuan and introduce it to the whole country, and arouse the interest of the Chinese people in developing Sichuan's industry. This is fortunate for the people of Sichuan and is also an essential plan for revitalizing the country. This time, I will do my best to investigate the current state of Sichuan's products and the hidden minerals, present them to the government, and publicize them to the people. I will also discuss plans with the Sichuan authorities to welcome investment from other provinces to save the country's economic decline. Sichuan is rich in minerals, especially oil. Exploration is already underway and drilling will begin soon. Our country's poverty is due to abandoning wealth on the ground. With concerted efforts, why worry about not being strong? The length of this trip is difficult to determine, but it will be measured by the task. I will do my utmost to fulfill the purpose entrusted by the authorities."

British Industrialists Visit China 196

Recently, there have been quite a few British industrialists visiting China. When the Empress of Britain arrived in Shanghai last week, there were two British industrialists among the passengers. After staying in Shanghai for a few days, they are now heading north to visit Tianjin and Beijing. The business practices of these two are worth noting and emulating by our Chinese people. They are as follows: Sir Watte, born in 1885, is the chairman of Bolton Textile Co. Ltd., located in Liverpool, England. Throughout his life, he has felt the importance of industrial and scientific training, and he has specially sent his son to study textile engineering at the University of Leeds. He has also donated 20,000 pounds to the University of Leeds and two other universities for chairs, and has employed graduates from these universities in his company. Mr. Knauf is also traveling with Sir Watte and is one of the most famous businessmen in Yorkshire. He has a large wool spinning factory near Bradford and founded the British Wool Research Association. He has occupied a large part of the influence in the work after its establishment. The association's annual expenditure is between 20,000 and 30,000. The importance of its nature can be known.

Memorial Monument for Awarding Women Greats 197

To Be Carved by Mr. Teng Baiye

The Women's Voice Society of this port, in order to celebrate its first anniversary and test the public's opinion on women greats, launched a women greats election last autumn. The deadline was 5:00 PM on December 29th, and a total of more than 1,700 votes were received. That evening, Huang Renzhi, Wu Xizhi, and other gentlemen were invited to supervise the counting of the votes at the Bankers' Association. The modern women greats were Soong Ching-ling, Xie Bingxin, Ding Ling, Liu Wang Liming, and He Xiangning. Everything has been recorded in previous newspapers. Now it is learned that the society has changed the prizes to a common marble memorial monument because the prepared prizes lacked public education. It has also invited modern art sculptors Teng Baiye, Li Zhongdao, and Liang Desuo to be the preparation committee. It has been heard that everything is ready. On the right side will be carved an ideal girl holding a torch in her hand, leading forward. The upper left corner will be inscribed with the four characters "Women's Role Models." The middle will be engraved with the names of the ten selected women greats. The lower left corner will write "Presented by the Women's Voice Society," and it will be carved by Mr. Teng Baiye. It is also heard that this gift will be completed by the end of this month and will be given to the most powerful organization in this city that promotes public education.

Maochang Cold Storage Nanshi Branch to Open 199

The No. 2 warehouse on the China Merchants Bureau's Jinliyuan Wharf (the old site is the base at No. 69 in the French Concession) was taken back by the Sandetang Company. The company then commissioned the Yong'an Real Estate Company, managed by the Sandetang Company, to plan and build a reinforced concrete warehouse. The project was completed in May of last year and was leased to Maochang Co., Ltd. for storing goods. The warehouse has a total of ten floors with a height of 160 feet from the ground to the top.

The Maochang Cold Storage in the Nanshi area, which will soon open, is the highest warehouse in Shanghai, with a volume of 460,000 cubic feet. It is heard that the company has recently installed refrigeration equipment on the lower four floors and used the latest American scientific methods to keep the goods fresh for a long time. At present, it is working day and night and is scheduled to officially open for business on April 1 to meet the needs.

China Stone Company Hosts Banquet for Shanghai Construction Industry 200

Our country is vast and rich in resources, especially in stone materials. However, the Chinese people often neglect to use these high-quality, beautiful stones. Mr. Yao Huasun, recognizing this, resolutely founded the China Stone Company in Qingdao and established a branch factory in Shanghai. Yesterday, Mr. Tao Guilin initiated an introduction to the construction industry, hosting a banquet at the Great Eastern Hotel at 6 PM to promote the recognition of domestic building stone materials. The guests filled the hall, creating a grand occasion. Mr. Tao delivered a speech, stating that the establishment of the Stone Company meets the needs of China's current construction industry and advocating for the use of domestic stone materials. Subsequently, Mr. Yao Huasun, the company's general manager, reported on the company's founding purpose and progress. Mr. Li Dachao from the Municipal Government also participated, expressing his enthusiasm for promoting domestic goods and delivering an inspiring and insightful speech. Other architects, including representatives from the Architectural Association, expressed their agreement and support. The company's exhibits included over 30 types of materials such as granite, jade Buddha stone, and marble. Besides building materials, there were also many exquisitely crafted art pieces on display, a dazzling array. Tests have shown that the quality of these materials is superior to imported products, setting a new record for domestic products.

Zhabei Third Section Fire Brigade Tests Taishan Brand Fire Extinguisher 201

Remarkable Results

Qingyun Industrial Factory, located at No. 12 Huacheng Road in the French Concession, has recently invented several types of Taishan brand foam fire extinguishers. The effectiveness was tested by the Zhejiang Provincial Government, which adopted them as aids for provincial fire protection. Major factories have also tested and purchased them, all praising their significant effectiveness. Yesterday, the 25th, the Zhabei Third Section Fire Brigade conducted a large-scale public demonstration at the intersection of Qiujiang Road and Guangdong Road. Chinese and foreign attendees were present to observe, creating a crowded and lively scene. First, a wooden house was erected on an open space, surrounded by flammable materials, and gasoline was poured inside and ignited. The fire blazed intensely. When the Taishan brand foam fire extinguisher was used to spray foam, the fire was immediately extinguished (in just 35 seconds). Simultaneously, a large iron bucket filled with gasoline and several pounds of cotton yarn was ignited for demonstration, resulting in an even fiercer fire. Upon spraying the foam, the fire was completely extinguished (in 58 seconds). Chinese and foreign attendees unanimously praised the remarkable effectiveness, setting a new record for fire extinguisher performance and proving it to be a valuable tool for fire protection.

Fire in a Building on Dajing Road, Nine Acres, One Person Burned to Death 202

Zhu Gaoming Careless with Fire

Yu Hu's Life Lost Instantly

Yesterday at 1:25 AM, a fire broke out in the room of Zhu Gaoming, who lived in the attic of Ms. Qian Shui's residence, a Ningbo woman, at No. 194 Dajing Road, Nine Acres. Due to carelessness with fire, the flames quickly spread, bursting through the roof. The Fire Brigade Joint Association sounded the alarm, and fire brigades from various districts rushed to the scene with pump trucks to extinguish the fire. By around 2 AM, the fire was extinguished. During the blaze, the Second District First Precinct dispatched officers to maintain order and took Qian Shui, the landlady, for questioning. It was learned that the building was also occupied by Yu Renfu, Zhu Gaoming, Liu Baolian, and Ms. Xi Jin. At the time of the fire, everyone was asleep. When they awoke and realized the danger, the smoke was overwhelming, and the fire was raging, leaving them with no escape. Fortunately, the firefighters bravely rescued Chen, Zhu Gaoming's wife, their eldest daughter Jufeng, their second daughter Jindi, and Hu, Yu Renfu's wife. However, Yu Hu suffered severe burns to her head and face and died instantly. The other injured individuals were sent to a hospital for treatment. The police precinct notified the local area head to report to the Shanghai Local Court, requesting officials to investigate. The fire destroyed one building, without affecting others.

City News 203

Tian Shen Copper and Iron Foundry Commences Operations: The Tian Shen Copper and Iron Foundry, located at No. 1054 Lujiabang Road, Nanshi, initiated by Le Shuzi and Li Xinglin, among others, has been in preparation for nearly a month. It officially commenced operations yesterday, smelting copper and iron. The various machine parts produced are said to be bright and of superior quality, ensuring suitability and satisfaction for all machine factories, whether custom-made or for replacement.

The Reputation of Yanhua Restaurant's Cantonese Cuisine: The Yanhua Restaurant, located west of Daxin Street on Fourth Avenue, has been established for over 30 years. In recent years, its business has been thriving. Previously, it only offered individual dishes. Now, there are several reservations for full-course meals daily. Dishes priced from ten to sixteen yuan would cost fourteen to twenty yuan elsewhere. Although the restaurant's facade retains its traditional style, its cuisine is highly popular among diners, mainly due to the freshness of the ingredients and reasonable prices.

Dahua Advertising Company Ready for Launch: Prominent figures in the business community, including Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Zhou Jianyun, and Pan Yousheng, recognizing that industry is in its infancy and domestic products are seeking development, see an urgent need for advertising agencies to meet the demands of the times. They have established Dahua Advertising Co., Ltd. to serve society and help various sectors achieve promotional effectiveness. A preparatory meeting was held last night at the Meiyuan Restaurant, attended by over ten people, including Wang Xiaolai, Pan Yousheng, Hu Die, Hu Shan, Shi Naixiu, Chen Haosheng, Wei Lingyun, and Jiang Donglai. The meeting approved the share prospectus and reported on business plans. The office is located on the fifth floor of the YWCA Building on Yuanyingmingyuan Road. It is said that business will commence soon.

Bargain Finds Amidst Huahua Silk Company's Big Discount Sale: Since launching its spring discount sale, the Huahua Silk Company, located at the corner of Shilu Road on Third Avenue, has seen exceptionally strong business due to the inclusion of aviation lottery tickets. Daily transactions have exceeded four to five thousand yuan. It is reported that the company, to reciprocate customers' patronage, has purchased a large quantity of new and fashionable silk fabrics in cash from major factories. Among them, the pulp-printed Qiu Man crepe is sold for 25 cents per foot, domestic flannel for 38 cents per foot, shimmering blue heron crepe for 38 cents per foot, and brocade-ground crepe for 48 cents per foot, making them the most affordable. With the arrival of bright spring weather, it is a good opportunity for everyone to acquire new outfits and enjoy themselves.

Midnight Snacks at the Paramount: The facilities at the Paramount Hotel are meticulously planned, and have long been well-known. This item is based on famous snacks from major hotels in Paris and the Monte Carlo Grand Casino, and is a unique offering in Shanghai. Ladies and gentlemen, after enjoying your evening, why not give it a try?

The Efficacy of Tang's Asthma Powder: Dr. Tang Feili, director of Tang's Asthma Specialist Hospital at No. 502 Continental Commercial Building, Nanjing Road, is renowned for his expertise in treating asthma. His creation, Tang's Asthma Powder, is also incredibly effective. This medicine has been tested for over ten years, curing countless patients and is the most effective oral medicine for asthma. According to those who have taken it, the medicine not only works quickly but also has no side effects such as vomiting, headache, or insomnia. The price is said to be only one yuan per box or ten yuan per dozen.

Medical Field 204

Effective Remedy for Throat Ailments: Since the beginning of spring this year, due to irregular weather patterns, throat ailments have become prevalent. Often, neglect leads to untreatable conditions. Although there are many throat specialists in Shanghai, the consultation fees are expensive, making it difficult for poor families to afford treatment. Recognizing this deeply, Mr. Zhao has acquired a type of natural throat-healing herb from his hometown. Over the years, he has gifted it to relatives and friends, and all who take it recover quickly. Through word of mouth, requests have been numerous. Now, to make it more accessible, he plans to widely distribute it to patients, charging a small fee of two yuan per box to cover the cost of the herbs. You can purchase it at Mr. Zhao's residence at No. 28 Songshan Road, French Concession. If truly impoverished, out of his desire to help the world, he will provide it free of charge upon request.

Painting and Calligraphy News 205

Minjiao Museum Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition: Mr. Chen Songchun, curator of the Shanghai Municipal Minjiao Museum, is promoting national culture by collecting numerous ancient and modern calligraphy and paintings at the museum starting January 1st. The works are divided into two sections for display. They include Cai Xiang's ancient post, Fang Huqing's ink dragon, and Li Zhihua's peony and bird paintings, all of which are excellent works. Visitors are extremely crowded, praising each other. The post includes "Litchi Records", "Tea Records", "Painting Jintang Records", and handwritten notes. Because of the changes in the mountains and the destruction of the tombs, this tablet has now been lost, so it is rarely seen. Fang's ink dragon cloud and mist use superb brushwork, and Li's peony and bird paintings are extremely rich and gorgeous, with birds facing each other, and the composition and coloring are top-notch. Both are from Wujin. How does Wujin's calligraphy and painting have such a unique advantage?

Weather Report 207

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the northeastern part of China is cloudy, with winds varying from southeast to northeast. There are northeast winds and fog in the surrounding areas of Shandong. The Yangtze River basin, this area, and the coastal area south of Ma'anshan Island are overcast with unstable light winds and fog or drizzle. There are cyclones and rain around Kyushu.
