Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Transformation of Relations Between the US and Japan 299

— Mingtang

Recently, what has caused a stir internationally is likely the transformation of relations between the US and Japan.

The transformation of relations between the US and Japan - how unexpected this is! The tension between the US and Japan did not begin today. Since the end of the Great War, the parallel development of American and Japanese capitalism has meant that the two imperialist powers have had extremely acute contact. This contact reached an unprecedented level of tension after the September 18th Incident two years ago. One side wanted to dominate East Asia exclusively; the other wanted to share East Asian interests, which meant that the United States wanted to occupy a position in the international division of East Asia, and a very important position at that. The excessive expansion of Japanese imperialism threatened to prevent the realization of this American attempt. This was, of course, absolutely intolerable to the United States. Therefore, Japan became the only obstacle to American development, and at the same time, the United States became the only target of Japanese struggle. Mutually opposed and mutually fighting, the tension in US-Japan relations created the only crisis of war in East Asia. The US-Japan war was on almost everyone's lips. As 1935 approaches in an instant, the issue of revising the London Naval Treaty and the issue of the Japanese mandated territory in the South Seas have become major hidden reefs in the future of the Pacific. It seemed that the contradiction between Japanese and American imperialism could never be resolved, and that a second world war would inevitably break out in East Asia first.

Unexpectedly, in this extremely tense atmosphere, there was news of a sudden transformation in US-Japan relations. What interesting and unexpectedly sudden news this is!

What exactly is being sold in the gourd regarding the transformation of US-Japan relations? In my opinion, this is nothing remarkable; at most, it is just another manifestation of the active war preparations of international imperialism!

How do you explain this?

First, we must know that we have already reached the eve of the Second World War. This war will inevitably destroy some of the great powers, or even all of them. So, how can we occupy a particularly advantageous position in the Second World War and avoid the fate of destruction? This has become a hot topic of discussion among the imperialist powers. They know that war is inevitable, but they are not willing to act rashly, because they know that in the next war, carelessness could lead to decline. The so-called "plan before you move," and now is the time for them to "plan." The reason why none of them are willing to start a fire for the time being is because the "plan" has not yet been "determined." Once the plan is determined, they will immediately start the war. This is one.

Since the current international political and economic situation is in the planning phase before the next world war, that is, in preparing for war, then the significance of the so-called understanding between Japan and the United States is also knowable. That is to say, the understanding between Japan and the United States is a manifestation of this "plan." How do we know this? Because the contradictions between Britain and the United States inevitably force the United States to divert some of its strength to deal with Europe; and the fact that "Manchuria and Mongolia" have not been actively "developed" and the existence of the state of opposition to the Soviet Union make it impossible for Japan to divert some of its strength to deal with the Soviet Union and "build" its so-called "Manchuria and Mongolia." In this way, the understanding between Japan and the United States becomes necessary. The reason why they want to understand each other is precisely for the sake of how to occupy a particularly advantageous position for themselves in the future war. Once preparations are completed, the war will begin. This is a definite fact. This is two.

Since the current world has reached the eve of war as a whole, and the so-called understanding between Japan and the United States is just another manifestation of the great powers' war preparations, then the future of the so-called understanding between Japan and the United States can be imagined. On the contrary, this is not a harbinger of peace, but a step further in promoting the world crisis.

Don't believe it? The world economic panic is deepening day by day. Where is the way out for the entire capitalist system? Except for war!

What is noteworthy is the position of China! As a result of the US-Japan understanding, I am afraid it is not a reconciliation between the two countries, but an agreement to divide China equally? Isn't that right? The first sound of the US-Japan understanding is that the United States is preparing to recognize the so-called "Manchukuo"!

A Model for Beggars 300

A few days ago, the private Wuxun Middle School in Tangyi County, Shandong Province, sent a commemorative volume of Mr. Wuxun. As a beggar, he was able to overcome the cold, hunger, and hardship to achieve his meritorious work in educating talents. He is truly worthy of being a good model for beggars. His brief biography and photo are printed below.

Portrait of Mr. Wuxun

Mr. Wuxun was born in a farmer's family in Wuzhuang, north of Tangyi City, Shandong Province. His family was poor. When he was a few years old, his father, Mr. Zongyu, passed away. He and his mother, Cui, and his elder brothers, Qianci and Rang, struggled to make a living. When he was just twenty years old, he was hired in other villages. He used the money he earned to buy delicious food for his mother. Sometimes, his master praised him for his hard work and gave him delicious food, which he would always bring back to his mother. Later, he was hired at his sister's house and served for several years. His sister's husband deceived him for his foolishness and concealed his wages. Mr. Wuxun did not argue with him and quit his job. He was then hired at the home of a student surnamed Mou in the northeast of Guantao City. From spring to winter, he was not paid his wages. Mr. Wuxun endured until the following year, but Mou was still the same, not paying him a penny and being harsh to him. Mr. Wuxun was very depressed. He lay in the mill room for several days without speaking or eating, and then quit his job. He seemed to be crazy. People would ask his name, but he would not answer and called himself "Justice of Righteous School."

In the early years of Tongzhi's reign, his mother passed away. He and his brothers lived separately. He only had three acres of land, which he sold for 120 strings of cash. Together with the money he had earned from hiring, he had a total of 210 strings of cash. He knew that Lou Junling of Guantao was virtuous, so he went to his door to ask him to manage the money for him, saying, "This is the money I earned from hiring to build a righteous school. Please do not refuse!" Mr. Lou did not know him and refused, but he knelt down and persisted, so he agreed.

From then on, he gave up hiring and became a beggar. Mr. Wuxun did not keep a braid. He only left hair on his forehead in the shape of a peach, and shaved it irregularly on the left and right sides. He wore a ragged cloak, carried a copper spoon, and wore a hundred-patched coat. He traveled through the city streets, calling out for work to make a living, or performing skills to earn money, or picking up broken threads and remnants to make thread balls. Over time, people knew Mr. Wuxun's personality and respected him very much. He often went in and out of the homes of ordinary people. Even women in their boudoirs did not avoid him. Therefore, he often acted as a matchmaker. If he begged for better food, he would sell it to get money. If he begged for scraps, he would eat it himself. If he had nothing, he would fill his stomach with vegetable roots and taro tails, or even snakes, scorpions, tiles, and pebbles. If someone gave him clean water to drink, he would wash his face first and then drink it. He went to great lengths to suffer himself, and accumulated wealth over the years.

Later, his accumulated wealth gradually increased, and he successively purchased land. Some people advised him to marry, but he firmly refused. He continued to beg and had no fixed place to stay. One night, he stayed in a dilapidated temple in Mijiatang Village. Unfortunately, a tile fell from the roof of the temple and injured his head. He still sang and encouraged himself. During the day, he went to the city and spoke in rhyme, like songs and poems, always advocating the creation of righteous schools.

In the early years of Guangxu's reign, he had accumulated tens of thousands of dollars, but his clothes were still worn and his food was still coarse. At this time, Mr. Wuxun used his accumulated wealth to purchase some red grain. His brother asked his neighbors to borrow money, but Mr. Wuxun refused. He leased the land he had purchased to his brother, but did not accept money. So, Mr. Xing quit his job. Also, Gao, a resident of Xierzhuang in Guantao, owed Mr. Wuxun more than 200 strings of cash in principal and interest. He repeatedly refused to pay and even threatened Mr. Wuxun to sue him. Mr. Wuxun decided not to ask for it anymore. In the winter of the twelfth year, he purchased more than 230 acres of land and asked Yang Shufang, a resident of Liulin Town, to recruit tenants to cultivate the land and manage the rest of his assets.

When Mr. Wuxun first proposed to build a school, he bought a house site in Wuzhuang, valued at 670 strings of cash. Because he felt that the situation was too narrow and feared that the Wu family would seize it in the future, he asked Mr. Yang to choose a school site in Liulin Town. Guo Junfen donated 1.8 acres of land outside the Dongwei Gate in the town. He built 24 houses and a gate and wall. It was completed in less than a month. He hired famous teachers to teach, and scholars gathered there. Every time Mr. Wuxun invited a teacher to the door, he would bow and greet him and treat him with a rich feast. If the teacher was tired and sleepy, he would kneel beside the bed. If the teacher returned to his hometown for some reason and was late returning to school, Mr. Wuxun would rush to his home day and night and kneel down to ask him respectfully. If a student was lazy, he would persuade him when others were not watching. If he did not listen, he would kneel down and beg him! Therefore, the diligence of teachers and students in the school was the best of the time. He expanded the righteous school to the neighboring counties. Mr. Wuxun became more diligent in accumulating wealth. Liao Zheng, a monk at the Qianfo Temple in Zhuangkecun, Guantao, admired Mr. Wuxun's character and donated all his savings. Therefore, he purchased more than 100 acres of land and a house in Yang Erzhuang, and built more than 10 houses. He hired teachers to teach as in the righteous school in Liulin. At that time, Guo Gong, the magistrate of Tangyi County, heard of Mr. Wuxun's name and invited him to the yamen to treat him to a feast. This was the first time in Mr. Wuxun's life that he had a good meal. Also, Yu De, a vice minister, came to Dong to inspect the school. Mr. Wuxun persuaded him to donate and he generously donated 200 taels of silver. With the support of the gentry in Linqing County, he purchased a house in Yushi Lane in Linqing City. Before the matter was completed, Mr. Wuxun passed away. Fortunately, Mr. Wang Pixian continued to operate and fulfilled Mr. Wuxun's legacy. When Mr. Wuxun was ill, his nephew Kexin went to see him, but Mr. Wuxun did not speak to him. Before his death, he still glared at him.

According to the records, Mr. Wuxun was born on the 19th day of the tenth month of the eighteenth year of Daoguang's reign at the hour of Mao (5-7 AM), and died on the 23rd day of the fourth month of the twenty-second year of Guangxu's reign at the hour of Wu (11 AM-1 PM). According to his will, he was buried outside the east wall of the righteous school he built in Liulin Town, Tangyi County. (Que Chou)

Women and Crying 301

— Dao

"Heroes don't shed tears lightly" - this indicates that a tough man does not cry easily, showing a heart of stone. However, women are different. Women are very prone to tears, especially in front of men. Women's tears are even more readily available. It is no exaggeration to say that women and crying are two-in-one. This is almost always the case.

Whenever women encounter unsatisfactory situations or excessive stimulation, they disregard everything and cry loudly, using crying as the only method of self-comfort. Men are not entirely the same. Under the same circumstances, they can only grit their teeth and endure in silence, trying to find a way to deal with the situation. This is not to say that men do not cry, but women cry much more often than men. Crying is not entirely a bad thing. When a person's mood is extremely depressed and cannot be vented, they always want to be able to cry loudly, as if all the sorrow and troubles can be cried out, and they will feel much more comfortable afterwards. This may have some physiological benefits, which may explain why people sometimes like to cry. However, women's particular fondness for crying, and the reason why women cry, in addition to the above reasons, has another meaning. This meaning is limited to the relationship between women and men. Under these circumstances, women's crying has an unbelievable magical power. Smart women use it as a portable treasure to deal with men. The saying "a woman's tears can melt a hero's heart" is clear evidence. We can often see between couples and lovers that when they argue about something, the woman cannot overcome the man, but is unwilling to back down or admit defeat. So, she releases her final weapon, collapsing on the bed and sobbing softly, or crying loudly in the presence of heaven and earth, tearfully telling her story as if she has been wronged, regardless of whether she is right or wrong. At this time, the man sees her pitiful and charming appearance. He cannot help but hate and love her at the same time, but the love is always greater than the hate. His hard heart is softened by the crying. He regrets causing trouble and needlessly stirring up a storm. So, not only will he automatically cancel his anger, but he will naturally approach the woman, stroke her hair, and comfort her with a humble attitude, saying a lot of nice things. Then, the victory belongs entirely to her, and the woman feels satisfied. So, she immediately turns from crying to laughter, and the tragicomic drama ends. Women's crying is really the best means of dealing with men, and also the most sharp and powerful method. Moreover, crying is originally very contagious. When you hear someone crying, you cannot help but feel sympathy or sadness for them, because people are all emotional, unless you are a piece of wood. Not to mention women's crying, which is rich in rhythm and gentle and tactful. No matter how heartless and unfeeling a man is, he will be moved by a woman's crying. Therefore, crying is a unique skill of women, a clever skill used to deal with men.

Fishing and Killing Family 302

— Meng

After Mr. Guo heard what Steward Ding said, he repeatedly said, "Yes!" He immediately took the account book and ran to Xiao En's house like a dog. This is exactly: "The rich raise slaves like dogs: they run as soon as they are called!" He only knows "obeying orders" and "submitting" in his life!

Mr. Guo arrived at Xiao's house: Xiao En greeted him respectfully, and Guiying quickly served tea; but he sat down rudely and spread out the account book with a fierce face to demand money. Xiao En pleaded repeatedly: he only allowed him to pay tomorrow; but interest must be added.

Spring Dream 303

— Xiao Qiao

Spring, intoxicating spring, last night's dream was too surprising.

Heavy rain hit the window, it was already dusk. I lay in the sofa chair chewing on Micoli candy, gazing absently at a spring fashion picture. Women are all lovely, with slender figures, wearing such narrow cheongsams, they raise their two lotus root-like fleshy arms, turn their heads, and wink at you, as if saying: "Love me, I am a youthful girl!"

Smiling, I lit a cigarette and also squinted one eye at her. She seemed to be laughing at me, laughing at me for not having enough courage, why not hug the girl you love tightly? Foolish, it's a picture. I flipped through, and picture after picture rolled before my eyes, those were such light and graceful girls.

"Girls are indeed beautiful,

Indeed they are light and graceful,

Indeed embracing her, kissing her,

Can comfort the fatigue of your life."

Holding the picture album, I closed my eyes, smoking a cigarette, listening to the rain, I seemed to be snuggling in my lover's arms, hypnotized.

The door opened, and that light and graceful girl wearing the clothes from the spring fashion picture, smiling and gazing at me, so charming. She stood still for a long time, seeing that I did not move, she stepped lightly with a waltz step, smiling even more charmingly. At this moment, I did not ask who she was, I stood up and hugged her. She leaned in my arms as if boneless, raised her head, slightly closed her long eyelashes, and a smile appeared at the corner of her mouth, she was waiting for me, waiting for me, for a passionate, intoxicating kiss.

However, I cannot be too presumptuous, towards a girl, one should gently caress and tenderly cherish, then kiss her, she will be grateful for your kindness. She remained for a long time, as if she had stopped breathing, she slightly opened her eyes, and met mine, she slightly closed them again.

Suddenly, a Roman warrior appeared before me at the door, he drew his sword and stabbed at me. The girl quickly broke free from my embrace, stood between the two of us, shook her head, looked at the warrior with resentment and glared at him, the warrior weakly retracted his sword, grabbed the girl's arm and walked out. The door slammed shut and I woke up from my dream.

Holding the spring fashion picture album in my arms, half a cigarette was smoldering in the ashtray, emitting a foul smell, the sound of rain on the window had not stopped, looking at the clock, it was only a five-minute dream, and I returned to this small room. I flipped through the picture album directly to the page with the girl, with the same appearance as in the dream, squinting her eyes at me, saying: "Love me, I am a youthful girl!"

I threw the spring fashion album maliciously onto the bed, the Roman warrior on the cover was drawing his sword and wrestling with someone. I laughed, picked up a Micoli candy and chewed it slowly.

New Annotations of Proverbs 305

— Wenguang

Many proverbs are circulating in our society. Although the words are crude, if we ponder them carefully, most of them coincide with recent events. If you don't believe me, let me first annotate the proverbs that are popular in our hometown one by one.

(1) A crooked mouth blowing a trumpet, a mass of evil.

Annotation: The clown Puyi usurped the throne and proclaimed himself emperor.

(2) A coffin on the city wall, a long detour.

Annotation: Russia sent the remnants of the Baltic Fleet to attack Japan.

(3) Carrying a stone mortar to tease a lion, exerting effort without pleasing.

Annotation: Handling the diplomacy of weak countries.

(4) A dragonfly biting its tail, eating itself.

Annotation: The struggle between the two Liu uncles and nephews in Sichuan.

(5) A crooked-headed monk chanting sutras, not matching the scriptures.

Annotation: The words when in opposition and the actions after taking office.

(6) Beating a copper drum with a meat bone, confused and noisy (smelly drumming).

Annotation: The clown's teacher, the eighty-six-year-old Chen Baozhen, sneaked off to Changchun.

(7) A Vajra soaring through the clouds, eight feet suspended in the air.

Annotation: Sun Chuanfang's Three Loves Doctrine and Zhang Zongchang's Outline for National Construction (both of which have been seen in newspapers).

(8) Taking a pulse on the thigh, extremely weak and exhausted.

Annotation: Loudly advocating entertainment to save the country and art to save the country.

(9) A six-fingered person telling fortunes, it won't be his turn.

Annotation: In the 1934 British Who's Who, there was no name of the German Chancellor Hitler or other leaders of the National Socialist Party government.

Film Special

A List of New Stars in 1934 307

— Huang Jiamo

The arrival of 1934 has brought about obvious changes. In the film industry of Europe and America, especially in the ever-changing Hollywood, the metabolism of stars, with new ones rising and old ones falling, has created a unique situation. The old stars, such as Mary Pickford, Gloria Swanson, and Douglas Fairbanks, have become figures of the past. 1934 has become an era for new stars to compete, although many veteran old stars can still maintain their original positions through continuous efforts, the novelty-seeking audiences have shifted their attention to those rising stars. The following are the lucky ones who have recently jumped onto the silver screen and won the audience's favor. They are now introduced separately as follows.

Mae West (Actress, Paramount) This charming and intelligent young woman possesses a sensitive mind and a uniquely stylish demeanor. She is a skilled screenwriter and has accumulated years of observation and experience, deeply understanding the demands of the general audience in the current century. She understands that this society is a man's world, and she has targeted men as her audience. This experiment has achieved unexpected success. Her two new works, "She Done Him Wrong" and "I'm No Angel," have won the amazement of the world (mostly men). The enthusiasm with which New York's Broadway welcomed her new films made many established stars both jealous and envious, and none were willing to attend. Now, she has become the idol of the general male audience.

Lee Tracy (Actor, Fox) Among the rising male stars, Lee Tracy is probably the most popular with audiences. However, he is not a handsome young man, nor does he excel at winning the hearts of women. Instead, he relies entirely on his lively performance and fluent eloquence to dominate the sound film industry. He is a typical figure in the busy metropolis of New York, with a brisk, straightforward, and refreshing performance style that forms a unique category, winning the enthusiastic love of English-speaking audiences. American film magazines often publish numerous letters from audiences praising him, which is evident. He has only been in the film industry for a short time, with works such as "Nuisance" and "Turn Back The Clock."

Dorothea Wieck (Actress, Paramount) She is a new actress recently brought to Hollywood from Germany. She revealed her great acting talent in the film "Madam in Uniform," representing a typical figure of noble chastity, a character that Hollywood lacks most. Her first starring film in the United States is called "Miss Fane's Baby is Stolen."

Jan Kiepura (Actor, British Gaumont) He is a famous singer in continental Europe, originally from Romania. However, the British promote him as if he were one of their own. In this year when musical films are warmly welcomed by the world, his world-renowned singing voice can naturally win general admiration. He made his debut in the film "Tell Me Tonight," creating a new box office record for European films. It was continuously shown in Shelley Wharf, Australia, for six months. The British also regard it as an honorary production of their country. His new film "City of Song" also achieved good results.

Franchot Tone (Actor, MGM) This handsome young man, dressed in the most fashionable clothes and enjoying extravagant material comforts, is a new figure. He is a typical American wealthy son, a representative of masculinity that white women dream of. Undoubtedly, he has been welcomed by the general female audience. He played the male lead in Joan Crawford's recent new film, "Dancing Lady." It is said that he is already Miss Crawford's lover. It is rumored that Miss Crawford's ex-husband, Douglas Fairbanks Jr., frankly criticized, "I can't find a man more handsome than Franchot Tone!"

Margaret Sullavan (Actress, Universal) This dreamy and beautiful girl only appeared fleetingly in "Only Yesterday," but her beautiful and extraordinary impression has been deeply imprinted in the hearts of the general audience.

Otto Kruger (Actor, 20th Century Fox) He is a popular star on the Broadway stage in New York. He began his screen career in 1933, making six films for 20th Century Fox in one year. He is an amiable middle-aged man, welcomed by the general audience for his profound performance.

June Knight (Actress, Universal) This beautiful and intelligent woman, as radiant as a peach blossom and as cold as ice, is one of the famous female performers on the Broadway stage in New York. She has only been in the film industry for a little over a year. After being promoted by Universal, she was first selected by the master director E.A. Dupont to play the lead role in "Ladies Must Love," and the results were indeed a sensation.

Film Reviews

Review of "Who is the Murderer?" 308

— Gaoyuan

"Matinee Idol" Guang Lu Lan Xin丨

This is the story of a famous actor being murdered out of jealousy.

Why is he envied? Without me saying it, nine out of ten people would guess that it is because of his "exceptional artistry" and "being worshiped by women." As a result, among the pursuers, love turns to hate, leading to the use of a gun to harm the person she loves most.

Such "romantic affairs" are common in modern society. Although the methods and processes of murder are different, the motives are the same. The social cause of this motive is undoubtedly capitalism. The private system of society is reflected in the relationship between men and women, forming an absolute demand for "exclusive possession" between men and women, requiring an extreme development of individualism, and this is what happens.

Here, I am reminded of the recent suicide of Chinese film actress Ai Xia. Although the causes of the motives are similar, fundamentally, failing to clearly recognize the social causes of the suffering and being unable to extricate oneself from the poison of the current society are the same. Social development has its future. People living in it cannot recognize and grasp its future and seek personal solutions, which is impossible.

The creative attitude of the screenwriter and director is still cautious, and they do not carelessly mix things up. A case of jealous murder is not treated like an absurd detective film. The famous actor's lover, Chriske, confesses to protect her sister, who is also her rival in love, Sarnia. In the end, Gotti, the female supporting role who is the murderer and also loves the famous actor, commits suicide by leaving a letter. All of this is possible in terms of emotions and reason. From the murderer's point of view, she is also committing suicide for love.

In addition to this main line, the insertion of Mrs. Cable, the famous actor's neighbor, provides the police with clues to the murderer, which is important, simple, and interesting. It adds a comedic atmosphere to the serious atmosphere, which does not destroy the overall atmosphere but strengthens the power of the whole play. Although most of Mrs. Cable's appearances are at the window, it is very natural. Until the last shot, she is still like an old woman, grumbling, which is not only interesting and gives the audience a natural and relaxed feeling, but also because this kind of character is real in life, this expression is appropriate.

Miles Mander's famous actor has the air of a swordsman. Whether in the foreground, backstage, or in daily life, his performance has the flavor of a "famous actor." Marguerite Allen is affectionate in her lively innocence. Nicola Keats wears black and white spotted clothes as soon as she appears on the stage, emphasizing her terrifying, sinister, and depressed character, and her expressions and movements also carry this meaning. Hay Petrie's male neighbor and Margaret Yarde's female neighbor fully express the characters of their roles through their expressions and movements.

The lighting, set design, and director George King can be matched according to the emotional development of the play, which emphasizes the effect of the play and shows his efforts. The dialogue throughout the play is very clear.

Review of "Bian Kun Gang" 309

— Ling He

丨丨 Guanghua Ying 丨丨

"Bian Kun Gang" is said to be Xu Zhimo's posthumous work, and the screenplay was written by Lu Xiaoman. Therefore, it has attracted considerable attention.

Regarding Xu Zhimo, we cannot deny his contributions to the Chinese literary world. Some people say that he is the representative of Chinese capitalist culture. In culture, we cannot forget Hu Shih, but in literature and art, we must mention Xu Zhimo. Indeed, he has made indelible achievements in introducing Western culture, but what he introduced was all decadent or beginning to decay. Such things are naturally more harmful than beneficial to China. Naturally, Xu Zhimo was a passionate romantic, which can be seen in his poetry. Even if he grasped reality, he distorted it due to incorrect observations, and therefore could not grasp the inevitable development of reality.

However, I regret to say that I have read very little about him, especially the script of "Bian Kun Gang," which I have never read. So now I can only express my humble opinions based on what is presented in the film. Of course, a literary work is often distorted by film merchants. In European and American films, we can cite many examples. Similarly, due to the different expression techniques of films, there are often many discrepancies between literary works, which is also an inevitable fact. Therefore, perhaps the original work is not as similar to the film as it seems. However, the screenwriter, Ms. Lu Xiaoman, should be responsible.

What exactly does "Bian Kun Gang" express? Perhaps it can be said that Bian Kun Gang is a stonemason, but he is an artist in the eyes of poets. After his wife's death, he loves his daughter, A Ming, extraordinarily, and does not want to remarry, lest a stepmother abuse his daughter. But the artist is a filial son. The subtitles say: Because his mother wants Ka Kun Gang to marry the newly widowed Li Qimei, but the picture tells us that he fell in love with Li Qimei after all, so he married her. Later, Li Qimei still refused to settle down as before and had relations with a shopkeeper. As a result, Ka Kun Gang's mother died of anger, and his daughter was blinded and killed by the adulterer and adulteress. Then the adulterer and adulteress eloped, and Ka Kun Gang committed suicide by jumping into a well in a fit of anger. At this time, his apprentice, filled with righteous indignation, wanted to avenge his master in the heavy rain. However, the mills of God grind slowly, yet they grind exceeding small. Li Qimei and the shopkeeper were struck to death by lightning in the woods, and the apprentice arrived, and there was no need to take action.

That's the story. Although a blind man is added to it, laughing coldly and mockingly, it makes people even more confused. I think this is unnecessary to explain. In the current Chinese films, there are still films that promote shallow loyalty, filial piety, and righteousness, and the vulgar karma of cause and effect, which is a strange phenomenon in the film industry.

Now let's see what the director has given us? Just give one example; after Li Qimei married Ka Kun Gang, why was she restless? How was she restless? And why did his mother die of anger? None of these are explained on the screen. In addition to rambling on and on in the instructions, our director just cleverly used a subtitle to end it.

As for the protagonist's performance, it is pretentious from beginning to end, with some of the flavor of an iron rooster and some of the flavor of singing civilized operas. The heroine has some merits of a rural woman in the first part, but the latter part is also not good. The others are self-evident.

"Flames" to be Released Tomorrow 310

Indeed, Yi Hua Film Company is bold!

Because large-scale films are rarely attempted in China, and Yi Hua Film Company's debut work, "The Fury of the Chinese Sea," is not only large-scale but also set in the vast ocean, which makes it even more magnificent. Now, another film more magnificent than "The Fury of the Chinese Sea" has been released, and this film is also produced by Yi Hua Film Company, which is "Flames," directed by Hu Rui and starring Peng Fei and Hu Ping.

The director of "Flames" is relaxed and sharp, the actors' expressions are calm and lively, and the photography is beautiful and novel. Everything about it is very extraordinary. This film has been approved by the Nanjing Film Inspection Committee and will be released at the Beijing Grand Theater tomorrow.

Silver Rain 311

— Ke Yuan

(1) Wang Yuanlong, recently, in view of the fact that American films of gods, ghosts, and horror are quite popular among the Chinese people, has put in a lot of effort and personally compiled an extremely terrifying script, named "The Strange Man in the Old House." (2) Wang Cilong's sound film "Spring Night Song" has now been directed by Wen Yimin, and the female lead is still the model beauty Ye Qiuxin, and the male lead is Qian Huafo. (3) Xue Juexian, after "The Amorous History of the Singing Stage," will direct another sound film, starring Xue himself and his wife Tang Xueqing. The name has been determined to be "Lover and Enemy." (4) Tang Jie will direct a fragrant, romantic, and amorous film, named "Red Lips," based on a script by Yu Dingxun, starring Hu Shan. (5) Tian Yi, usually a basketball player, recently had a whim and replaced rugby with basketball. Every afternoon, he plays rugby on the basketball court, which is very funny and comical, and the spectators' stomachs are aching with laughter.

Film Novel

Carolina (4) 312

— Wen Yin

"Are women obedient in the North?" Will asked incredulously. He thought, can a person freely choose between the South and the North? Joanna smiled and asked, "You hate the North the most, don't you?" Will said seriously, "They destroyed us!" Joanna said, "You weren't even born at that time. Mr. Will, your memory is really strong!" Will was a little annoyed, and he said, "You think that's good, don't you?" Joanna said, "Why do you care so much?" Will was very unhappy in his heart, but he still pretended to smile on the outside and said, "Okay, today's lesson is over." Joanna jumped down from the fence and said, "The lesson is over, the teacher can go home." Will quickly stopped her and said, "Don't go. You're right, Joanna; I'm very sorry. Now we'll just laugh it off." Joanna smiled at him slightly. Will urged her, "Why don't you laugh? Have you forgiven me?" So they laughed heartily and patrolled the tobacco in the field together.

Many of the early plantings were her father's handiwork and are now in bloom. Joanna smelled the fragrance of the tobacco flowers and praised them repeatedly. Will said, "Honestly, we don't like growing tobacco." Joanna glanced at him and said, "You don't grow anything at all. The fields are full of weeds." Will said, "That's all because we don't have money. Thanks to the North, they are determined to harm the South... Has your grandmother told you?" Joanna said, "No, she said that both sides were wrong in the North-South War." Will said, "I'm afraid your grandmother doesn't like Southerners, does she?" Joanna said, "No. She was originally going to marry a Southerner. Later, that person died in battle, so she ran to the North and married my grandfather. But she never forgot her first love for the rest of her life." Will thought that Florence was coming soon, so he said, "A person's marriage rarely allows them to be their own master." Joanna said, "Then why do people get married at all?" Will said, "There are many reasons... money is one of them..." Joanna said angrily, "Money? You don't need to sacrifice your happiness for money. You just need to work hard yourself." Will grabbed her arm and jumped over a field bank, and then said, "You are a very special person. Please tell me, how can you cultivate a field like this without money?" Joanna said, "Put all the fields together and tidy them up..." Will waved his hand and laughed before she could finish, "Plant a large area of tobacco!" Joanna said, "Do you think it's funny? I don't think it's funny. Growing tobacco is extremely profitable." Will was still joking, "A man can only smoke one cigarette at a time. Who will use so much tobacco that you grow? Do you even call women to smoke?" Joanna laughed and said, "That's also possible. You don't know, the tobacco I grow is originally for making cigarettes."

As they were arguing vigorously, Robert came forward and called Will to the station to meet Florence. So Will said goodbye to Joanna unhappily and left. Joanna sat down on the field bank, and unconsciously felt something in her heart, her eyes staring blankly at Will's receding figure. (To be continued)
